## Why adam

adam is a **deterministic cognitive kernel for Kazakh** ‚ÄĒ rule-based dialog with auditable belief revision, morpheme-indexed retrieval, and a forward-chaining reasoner over typed facts, all running as a single tool-driven pipeline. It trades **generalisation for integrity**: every output is traceable, every belief revisable, every conclusion sourced. Every layer is **Rust-only** and **graph-first** by repository invariant ‚ÄĒ both enforced by contract tests.

### Architecture name ‚ÄĒ ARK (Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel)

**v4.55.5+** ‚ÄĒ adam's architecture is named **ARK** = Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel. Renamed from NLM (Nano Language Model) to mark adam's distinct architectural class: not a smaller LLM, but a different kind of system entirely. The four pillars:

- **A**gglutinative ‚ÄĒ Kazakh morphology decomposes deterministically (root + typed suffixes); composition is rule-bound, not learned.
- **R**easoning ‚ÄĒ a curated knowledge graph (`data/world_core/*.jsonl`) + a forward-chaining reasoner (10 active rules) produces every fact-bearing claim. Every output cites a source.
- **K**ernel ‚ÄĒ system-runtime, not a probabilistic estimator. ARK has small trained components (selection-weights perceptron, suffix-chain priors, root-affinity PMI) but they sit inside the kernel as inspectable layers, not at the centre.

Tiny ML lives, large ML doesn't: the trained perceptron is 24 bytes / 6 f32; suffix priors and root affinity are statistical but auditable. Generation is template-based, never free-text. Result: predictable, traceable, watch-battery-deployable Kazakh dialog.

### Engineering thesis

The project's core engineering claim ‚ÄĒ independent of any historical or philosophical thesis about Kazakh ‚ÄĒ is that **agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning**: every Kazakh word decomposes into a root plus a sequence of typed suffixes, each contributing a known grammatical operator (case, number, tense, person, possessive, polarity, modality). Composition is rule-bound, not learned. That structure is exactly what we build the runtime on: FST morphology + typed suffix priors + root-pair PMI as deterministic prior layers, world_core as a curated graph of typed facts, and templates as the only path from fact to text. No probabilistic free generation. No retrained-from-scratch behaviour per release. The result is **predictable, traceable, low-energy** answer for Kazakh queries ‚ÄĒ not because the language has special metaphysical status, but because its structure is unusually friendly to formal modelling. The same engineering style would apply to other agglutinative-typology languages (Turkish, Kyrgyz, Tatar, Uzbek, ‚Ä¶) without claims of universal grammar.

¬ę–Ę–į–Ĺ—č—Ā–į–Ļ—č“õ.¬Ľ ‚Üí "**–ė”ô, ”ô—Ä–ł–Ĺ–Ķ. –ú–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ “õ–į–∑–į“õ—ą–į —Ā”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—É–≥–Ķ –į—Ä–Ĺ–į–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ ARK, –į—ā—č–ľ –į–ī–į–ľ.**". **(1)** `SystemIdentity::canonical()` updated: `full_name = "Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel"`, `abbreviation = "ARK"`. **(2)** Latin-token whitelist in `quality.rs` extended with Agglutinative/Reasoning/Kernel/ARK; **v4.55.0 ‚ÄĒ Metrics-currency CI gate (closes Codex's last hygiene gap).** v4.52.5 manually fixed ~15 numeric/version drifts across docs that had silently accumulated across 15 minor versions. v4.55.0 codifies that audit as an automated CI gate so drift can't reaccumulate. Each subsequent release either updates docs OR fails this gate. **(1)** New `scripts/check_metrics_currency.sh` ‚ÄĒ POSIX shell, depends only on jq + awk + grep + sed. 9 cross-checks against canonical artefacts: intent count (intent.rs enum vs README badge), world-core entries (jsonl line count vs README + data/README.md + world_core/README.md), total facts (retrieval/facts.json vs same 3 docs), workspace version (Cargo.toml vs README + performance.md header), informational reports (world-core .jsonl raw facts + derived facts count). Fails on first drift; error message names file + claim + live value. **(2)** Wired into `scripts/validate_foundation.sh` as a final post-test step ‚ÄĒ foundation validation now also gates on docs currency. **(3)** CONTRIBUTING.md pre-push checklist updated: replaces previous "manual README audit" bullet with the automated gate. **v4.46.5 ‚ÄĒ Stage B bundle 4 ‚ÄĒ production trace-wiring (audit-only).** First production touch in the Stage B arc. v4.45.0‚Äďv4.46.0 built the substrate (foundation + training + canonical pairs + audit primitive) entirely off-path. v4.46.5 wires the audit primitive into the live `tool::search_graph` dispatch ‚ÄĒ when 2+ admissible candidates, run `selection::audit_compare` against the heuristic top-1 and push a trace line if the trained selector disagrees. **No behavioral change** ‚ÄĒ the heuristic still wins; the trace is read by `--trace` consumers to surface where the selector would diverge. **Architectural significance:** first time selection-weights infrastructure runs in production on real corpus facts. With `default_v0()` weights (hand-set to approximate v4.38.0 tiers), disagreement should be rare; each surfaced disagreement is a candidate for the v4.47.0+ training corpus. **(1)** Audit-only wiring in `tool::search_graph` ‚ÄĒ admissible-candidate guard + `audit_compare` call + trace push on disagreement (silent on agreement). **(2)** Trace-only architectural pattern (mirrors v4.42.0 NLG parallel-path). **(3)** `query_tokens` propagation reuses the v4.38.0 list-aware ranker's vec. **(4)** `last_topic` deferred to `None` (recency feature scores 0 for both candidates; tier collapses to no-op until v4.47.0+ ToolContext extension). **Verification:** Workspace **946 passing** unchanged; adam-dialog 279 passing; selection module 34/34; live REPL byte-identical to v4.46.0; foundation unchanged; fmt + check clean. Cadence: `.5` ‚ÄĒ first Stage B production-side touch + audit-only architectural pattern. **Stripe (11) ‚ÄĒ generative AI via agglutinative composition.**

**v4.46.0 ‚ÄĒ Stage B bundle 3 ‚ÄĒ canonical gold pairs + audit substrate.** Two architectural primitives connecting the v4.45.5 training algorithm to the future v4.46.5+ production wiring. **(1)** `canonical_training_pairs_v0()` ‚ÄĒ 15 hand-curated `(positive, negative)` gold pairs covering 5 feature dimensions (confidence axis √ó 3, subject-overlap √ó 3, object-overlap √ó 1, recency √ó 2, richness √ó 1, multi-signal interactions √ó 5) + the disambiguation scenarios that the v4.38.0 SearchGraph ranker tiers handle today. Pure deterministic constant. Train `default_v0()` on this set with `train_perceptron` and the resulting weights satisfy every canonical scenario by construction. **(2)** `AuditResult` struct + `audit_compare()` ‚ÄĒ pure-function side-by-side comparison of "what the heuristic ranker picked" vs "what the trained selector would pick" given the same candidate list. Returns `{ heuristic_top_idx, selector_top_idx, disagreement: bool, score_gap: f32 }`. Stable-tie-break matches `select_top` semantics. **(3)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(4)** 10 new unit tests verify canonical-pair determinism / well-formedness / convergence / post-training rank correctness; audit agreement-vs-disagreement + score-gap reporting; degenerate-input handling. **(5)** No production wiring ‚ÄĒ pure infrastructure for v4.46.5+ trace integration. **Verification:** Workspace **946 passing** (was 936; +10 new audit tests); adam-dialog lib **279 passing** (+10); selection module 34/34 (13 + 11 + 10); canonical training pairs converge; live REPL byte-identical to v4.45.5; foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. Cadence: minor ‚ÄĒ Stage B bundle 3 (substrate for bundle 4 production routing + bundle 5 ranker replacement). **Stripe (11) ‚ÄĒ generative AI via agglutinative composition.**

**v4.45.5 ‚ÄĒ Stage B bundle 2 ‚ÄĒ pairwise margin-perceptron training pipeline.** Stage B continues. v4.45.0 shipped the foundation; v4.45.5 ships the training algorithm: pairwise margin perceptron that takes gold `(positive, negative)` candidate pairs and tunes `SelectionWeights` until every pair satisfies `score(positive) ‚Č• score(negative) + margin` (or `max_epochs` elapse). Pure function, deterministic per `(initial, pairs, config)`. **Architectural fit:** discrete (no gradient graph, no library deps), inspectable (still ~28 bytes after training), deterministic (no random sampling). Satisfies the thesis: ¬ęweights/learning OK if discrete, inspectable, cheap; reject only LLM internals¬Ľ. **(1)** `TrainingPair` struct (positive vs negative gold pair). **(2)** `TrainingConfig` with `learning_rate / margin / max_epochs` (default_v0: lr=0.1, margin=0.5, max_epochs=200). **(3)** `TrainingStats` reports `epochs_run / final_violations / converged`. **(4)** `train_perceptron(initial, pairs, config)` ‚ÄĒ the loop; per-epoch iterates pairs; failing pairs trigger update by `lr √ó (pos ‚ąí neg)` per weight component; early-exit on zero violations. **(5)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(6)** 11 new unit tests verify convergence on linearly-separable data, determinism, no-op when pre-converged, max-epoch reporting, empty-pair handling, single-dimension signal pickup (recency / confidence), zero-lr no-progress, multi-signal convergence, post-training rank correctness, stats reporting. **(7)** Not yet ‚ÄĒ real training data extraction from evals, audit-only wiring, production routing. **Verification:** Workspace **936 passing** (was 925; +11 training tests); adam-dialog lib **269 passing** (+11); selection module 24/24; live REPL byte-identical (no wiring yet); foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. Cadence: `.5` ‚ÄĒ 5 distinct innovations + kernel-signature algorithm. **Stripe (11) ‚ÄĒ generative AI via agglutinative composition.** Next: v4.46.0 ‚ÄĒ bundle 3 (real training data + audit-only wiring); v4.50.0 ‚ÄĒ trained-weights replacement of heuristic ranker.

**v4.45.0 ‚ÄĒ Stage B opens ‚ÄĒ selection weights foundation.** Stage B architectural milestone ‚ÄĒ first patch. The substrate for the project's stated path to LLM-comparable abilities without LLM costs. New `crates/adam-dialog/src/selection.rs` (~390 lines + 13 tests) defines tiny inspectable feature-weight tables that, in subsequent Stage B patches, will pick among rule-generated candidate responses. **Architectural significance:** Stage A built typed primitives + rule-based NLG + 46 curated domains; **Stage B starts here:** selection among candidates. Each weight is a single number in a table, readable by any human, deterministic per seed, no softmax sampling. **(1)** New `selection` module ‚ÄĒ `CandidateFeatures` (5 hand-extracted features: confidence / raw_text richness / subject overlap / object overlap / recency match), `SelectionWeights` (6 numbers + bias = ~28 bytes for v0), `extract_features`, `score`, `select_top` (stable-tie-break by first index for byte-identical regression). **(2)** Confidence mapping ‚ÄĒ `HumanApproved ‚Üí 1.0` / `CuratedQuote ‚Üí 0.8` / `RuleInferred ‚Üí 0.5` / `RepeatedPattern ‚Üí 0.3` / `Grammar ‚Üí 0.0`. **(3)** Token overlap ‚ÄĒ query tokens (‚Č• 3 chars, casefold) matching the slot root. **(4)** 13 new unit tests (deterministic feature extraction + correct scoring + stable selection). **(5)** Re-exports in `lib.rs`. **(6)** Foundation-only ‚ÄĒ no production wiring (mirrors v4.42.0 NLG-foundation pattern). **Verification:** Workspace **925 passing** (was 912; +13 new selection tests); adam-dialog lib **258 passing** (was 245; +13); selection 13/13; live REPL byte-identical (no production wiring); fmt + check clean. **v4.43.9 ‚ÄĒ `multiword_entity_hint` inflected-FIRST-word pass (architectural cleanup).** Closes the v4.43.8 architectural carry-forward. v4.43.8 fixed the ¬ę“ö–į–∑—Ė—Ä–≥—Ė “ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ –Ņ—Ä–Ķ–∑–ł–ī–Ķ–Ĺ—ā—Ė¬Ľ routing by registering both bare-form AND Gen-form variants of office phrases as multiwords ‚ÄĒ solved the symptom, but registering parallel Gen-form variants is data-drift waiting to happen. v4.43.9 lifts the fix to the matcher itself: a **third pass** in `multiword_entity_hint` detects inflected-FIRST-word forms via the six Kazakh genitive suffixes (-–Ĺ—č“£ / -–Ĺ—Ė“£ / -–ī—č“£ / -–ī—Ė“£ / -—ā—č“£ / -—ā—Ė“£), so future 2-word multiword entries no longer need parallel Gen-form registration. **v4.43.0 ‚ÄĒ Stage A bundle 3 ‚ÄĒ Introducer migration into NLG production path.** Stage A architectural milestone closing the deferred carry-forward from v4.42.6. **v4.42.0 ‚ÄĒ Stage A opens ‚ÄĒ rule-based NLG over typed semantic frames (foundation).** Opens **Stage A** of the project's refined thesis: adam as a NEW class of generative AI that uses the agglutinative paradigm ‚ÄĒ typed primitives + rule-based composition + tiny selection weights ‚ÄĒ to be safe / cheap / predictable while reaching LLM-comparable abilities. Templates were the rough draft; rule-based NLG over typed `SentenceFrame`s is the proper architecture. **(1)** New `crates/adam-dialog/src/nlg/` module with `render_sentence(frame) -> Option<String>` public API. **(2)** `SentenceFrame` typed wrapper ‚ÄĒ `{fact, mood, introducer}` mirrors agglutinative pattern (root + operators). **(3)** `NlgRule` trait ‚ÄĒ pluggable rule shape; trait-object polymorphism for community contributions. **(4)** 5 starter rules covering most-frequent factoid response patterns: IsA copula declarative (¬ęX ‚ÄĒ Y¬Ľ), PartOf declarative, HasQuantity (reuses curated raw_text), RelatedTo list-summary, LivesIn declarative. **(5)** 7 unit tests covering each rule path + Direct/AboutTopicFirst/OnTheSubjectMain/BrieflyAbout introducer variants + unknown-predicate fallthrough. **(6)** In-flight regression fix: ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–Ĺ—č“£ –Ī–į—Ä–Ľ—č“õ –į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ—ā–į—Ä—č–Ĺ —ā—Ė–∑—Ė–ľ–ī–Ķ“£—Ė–∑¬Ľ was returning notable-people list instead of –ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā—ā–į—Ä list ‚ÄĒ `“õ–į–∑–į`-prefix false-positive in direct_overlap; skip-list extended; —Ā–ł–Ĺ–ĺ–Ĺ–ł–ľ path correctly identifies –ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā—ā–į—Ä. **Stage A status:** v4.42.0 lays the foundation; NLG runs as parallel path (templates unchanged); subsequent v4.42.x will migrate template families to rules; ~v4.50 opens **Stage B** (tiny selection weights). **Verification:** Workspace **884 passing** (+7 NLG tests); regression fixed; anti-regression on all controls; fmt clean. User-explicit feature ask. **(1)** `try_evaluate_kazakh_word_math` evaluator ‚ÄĒ pipeline: detect math op via stem-prefix match (`–ļ”©–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—ā*` / `–Ī”©–Ľ*` / `“õ–ĺ—Ā*` / `–Ķ—Ā–Ķ–Ņ—ā–Ķ*` + closed inflected-form set for `–į–Ľ`-subtract); extract operand chunks using case-morphology as separator (Acc/Dat/Abl explicit case closes a chunk); compute integer; `None` on overflow / non-integer division. **(2)** Math-verb detection ‚ÄĒ switched to stem-prefix match catching all bare imperatives / converbs / conditionals; sentence-final-position rule for bare ¬ę–į–Ľ¬Ľ (math sense, distinct from sentence-initial conjunction). **(3)** Number-word parser ‚ÄĒ recognizes 0-9 / tens / 100 / 1000 / 10‚Ā∂ / 10‚ĀĻ in bare AND case-suffixed forms; composes compounds (¬ę–∂“Į–∑ –Ķ–Ľ—É¬Ľ = 150, ¬ę–Ī—Ė—Ä –ľ—č“£ —ā–ĺ“ď—č–∑ –∂“Į–∑ —ā–ĺ“õ—Ā–į–Ĺ —ā–ĺ“ď—č–∑¬Ľ = 1999, ¬ę–Ķ–ļ—Ė –ľ—č“£¬Ľ = 2000). **(4)** Case-morphology operand separator (compound numbers vs separate args). **(5)** `render_kazakh_number_words` ‚ÄĒ inverse renderer (0‚Ä¶999_999_999 ‚Üí canonical Kazakh phrase) surfaced alongside digit via `__math_words__` slot. **(6)** Math template family extended with `{math_words}` slot. **(7)** Lexicon coverage batch ‚ÄĒ 7 new entries (–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā / —Ä–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—É–Ī–Ľ–ł–ļ–į / –ľ–į“õ—Ā–į—ā / —Ā–Ņ–ĺ—Ä—ā / –≤–ł–ī–Ķ–ĺ / –į–Ľ“ď–į—ą“õ—č / –∂–į—ā—č—Ä). Coverage **85.28 % ‚Üí 86.21 %** (+0.93 pp). Cumulative v1.5.5 ‚Üí v4.41.0: **79.48 % ‚Üí 86.21 %** (+6.73 pp). **Verification:** Workspace **877 passing** (+12 from v4.39.7 baseline 865; 5 new word-math tests, 7 case-suffix synthesis tests); anti-regression on discourse anaphora preserved; foundation 1754 entries / 1920 facts / 39 domains / 25 501 derivations; fmt clean. ACCUSATIVE migrated to `{N}` archiphoneme. Vanilla `{D}` preserved for Loc/LocAttr. **(2)** 7 new synthesis-direction case tests (Gen on nasal/vowel/liquid/voiceless, Acc on nasal/vowel, Abl on nasal). **(3)** `genitive_topic_hint_for_list` simplified to parse-stream (was string-level workaround in v4.39.0; now uses FST-derived Genitive directly). **(4)** 11 high-frequency lexicon entries: –Ī–į—Ā / –Ī–Ķ—ā / –ľ–į–Ľ / –ĺ—Ä—ā–į / –ĺ—Ä—č—Ā / –Ņ–į–Ļ–ī–į / “õ–ĺ–Ľ / —Ā”©–∑ / –Ī–į—Ā—ā–į / –ĺ—ā—č—Ä / –ĺ—Ä–Ĺ–į–Ľ–į—Ā. **(5)** `deterministic_segment_parse` ‚ÄĒ fewest-segment-preference disambiguates root-collision ambiguity (frozen postpositions like ¬ę–Ī–į—Ā“õ–į¬Ľ win over compositional ¬ę–Ī–į—Ā + “õ–į¬Ľ; truly compositional forms still segment normally). **(6)** Morpheme coverage **83.27 % ‚Üí 85.28 %** (+2.01 pp); cumulative v1.5.5 baseline ‚Üí v4.39.7: **79.48 % ‚Üí 85.28 %** (+5.80 pp). **(7)** Bonus: ¬ę–ź–ī–į–ľ–Ĺ—č“£ –ľ–į“õ—Ā–į—ā—č –Ĺ–Ķ?¬Ľ / ¬ę–°”©–∑ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ď–į—Ā –ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ –Ĺ–Ķ?¬Ľ now correctly resolve to bridge facts. **Verification:** Workspace **872 passing** (+7 new case-suffix tests); 13 case-form roundtrip OK; bug 4 preserved via FST parse-stream; tokenizer 464/464 exact match; fmt clean. **v4.38.0 ‚ÄĒ Quantity-aware ranker + subject-synonym fallback + 53 role-bridge facts.** First minor in v4.38+ arc. Closes the v4.37.5 deferred bug 1 (HasQuantity ranking) and lays infrastructure for the v4.38.5 lexicon-cleanup arc that will close bug 4. **Before:** ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į ”©–∑–Ķ–Ĺ –Ī–į—Ä?¬Ľ ‚Üí "“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į 3 —Ä–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—É–Ī–Ľ–ł–ļ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ľ–į“£—č–∑—č –Ī–į—Ä “õ–į–Ľ–į –Ī–į—Ä: –ź—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–į, –ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č, –®—č–ľ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—ā." (cities ‚ÄĒ wrong). **After:** "**“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į –∂–Ķ—ā—Ė –ľ—č“£–Ĺ–į–Ĺ –į—Ā—ā–į–ľ ”©–∑–Ķ–Ĺ –Ī–į—Ä.**" Same shape works for –ļ”©–Ľ / —ā–į—É / “Ī–Ľ—ā—ā—č“õ —Ā–į—Ź–Ī–į“õ / –į—É—č–Ľ. **(1)** New `quantity_object_match_rank` tier in SearchGraph ‚ÄĒ when query has ¬ę“õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į/–Ĺ–Ķ—ą–Ķ¬Ľ, a HasQuantity fact whose `object.root` matches a content token wins; 3-char floor admits short content nouns (–ļ”©–Ľ, —ā–į—É, –Ķ–Ľ, –į—É—č–Ľ). **(2)** Reverse-guard demotes HasQuantity facts to rank 3 when no quantity intent ‚ÄĒ prevents new quantity facts hijacking type-list queries (¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č ”©–∑–Ķ–Ĺ–ī–Ķ—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?¬Ľ still surfaces RelatedTo list). **(3)** `SUBJECT_SYNONYMS` lookup fallback in SearchGraph ‚ÄĒ 4 pairs (–į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ‚ÜĒ–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā, –ļ—Ė—Ā—Ė‚ÜĒ–į–ī–į–ľ, —ā“Ī–Ľ“ď–į‚ÜĒ–į–ī–į–ľ, –Ķ–Ľ‚ÜĒ–ľ–Ķ–ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—ā); strictly defensive (fires only when direct lookup empty); preserves pre-v4.38.0 behavior bit-for-bit. **(4)** 53 new world_core facts in `role_bridges.jsonl` ‚ÄĒ 48 IsA bridges (–Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ą–Ķ—Ā—Ā–ł–ł‚Üí–į–ī–į–ľ/–ľ–į–ľ–į–Ĺ/—ą—č“ď–į—Ä–ľ–į—ą—č–Ľ—č“õ —ā“Ī–Ľ“ď–į; geography classes‚Üí–∂–Ķ—Ä –Ī–Ķ–ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė/–Ķ–Ľ–ī—Ė –ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ/”ô–ļ—Ė–ľ—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –Ī”©–Ľ—Ė–Ĺ—Ė—Ā) + 5 HasQuantity facts on natural geography. Per `project_bridge_fact_leverage`: each bridge multiplies R1 transitivity output. Reasoner derivations 24k ‚Üí **25 435** (+6 % from 53-fact addition). **(5)** `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` += 8 compound bridge objects. **(6)** `LIST_TYPE_SYNONYMS` += –Ī–į–Ľ–į‚ÜĒ“Ī–Ľ / “õ–į–Ľ–į‚ÜĒ–ľ–Ķ–≥–į–Ņ–ĺ–Ľ–ł—Ā / –Ķ–Ľ‚ÜĒ–ľ–Ķ–ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—ā / –ļ—Ė—Ā—Ė‚ÜĒ–į–ī–į–ľ / —ā“Ī–Ľ“ď–į‚ÜĒ–į–ī–į–ľ. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; all 7 quantity classes (”©–∑–Ķ–Ĺ/–ļ”©–Ľ/—ā–į—É/“Ī–Ľ—ā—ā—č“õ —Ā–į—Ź–Ī–į“õ/–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā/“õ–į–Ľ–į/–į—É—č–Ľ) route correctly; anti-regression on type-list queries; foundation validation **1750 entries / 1916 facts** clean; fmt clean. **v4.37.5 ‚ÄĒ Human-like clarification on low-confidence topic extraction.** First behavioural release in v4.37+ arc. Closes a real-REPL pattern from the 2026-05-03 transcript: when topic extraction recovered only a fallback candidate (an adjective surfaced as `Analysis::Noun`, or a deverbal participle that registers as `noun` in the lexicon), the response asserted a tangential fact about that candidate confidently. Pre-fix the system either echoed the wrong word or cited a corpus quote about a modifier the user clearly meant as a qualifier. **Before:** ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–Ĺ—č“£ –į—ā–į“õ—ā—č –∂–į–∑—É—ą—č–Ľ–į—Ä—č–Ĺ –į—ā–į“£—č–∑¬Ľ ‚Üí "–ź—ā–į“õ—ā—č ‚ÄĒ –į—ā–į“õ-–į—ā–ĺ–Ľ—É –į—Ą—Ą–ł–ļ—Ā—Ė..." (confident definition of an adjective). **After:** "–°—Ė–∑ –į—ā–į“õ—ā—č –∂–į–Ļ—č–Ĺ–ī–į —Ā“Ī—Ä–į–Ņ –ĺ—ā—č—Ä—Ā—č–∑ –ī–Ķ–Ņ “Ī“õ—ā—č–ľ. –Ē“Ī—Ä—č—Ā —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ľ –Ī–Ķ? –Ę–ĺ–Ľ—č“ď—č—Ä–į“õ –į–Ļ—ā—Ā–į“£—č–∑ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į–ī—č." (clarify, invite correction). **(1)** New `TopicConfidence` enum on `Intent::Unknown.noun_hint_confidence` ‚ÄĒ fifth analytical signal (after polarity, modality, evidence, inversion-question). **(2)** Two-pass `first_noun_root_with_confidence` prefers `part_of_speech == "noun"` AND demotes deverbal participles ending in `-“ď–į–Ĺ/-–≥–Ķ–Ĺ/-“õ–į–Ĺ/-–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ` (closes ¬ę—ą—č“õ“õ–į–Ĺ¬Ľ hijacking topic over ¬ę—ā“Ī–Ľ“ď–į¬Ľ). **(3)** Confidence-aware `best_noun_hint_with_confidence` threads the band through every extraction strategy. **(4)** Discourse-anaphora promotes confidence to High after substituting prior topic (preserves multi-turn anaphor list-class continuation). **(5)** Planner: `Low` confidence ALWAYS routes to `unknown.clarify_low_confidence` (even with retrieval evidence ‚ÄĒ corpus citation about an adjective is noise, not signal); `noun_hint == None` AND no_evidence ‚Üí `unknown.clarify_no_topic` (replaces bare ¬ę–Ę“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ī–Ķ–ī—Ė–ľ¬Ľ). **(6)** Two new template families ‚ÄĒ `unknown.clarify_low_confidence` (5 templates) + `unknown.clarify_no_topic` (5 templates) ‚ÄĒ purely meta-conversational, surface inferred subject and hand the next turn back. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; live REPL bugs 2/3 fixed; gibberish now hedges; greetings/name/confident-fact controls unchanged; anaphor list-class continuation preserved; fmt clean; live latency 0.33 s / 176 MB (within v4.37.0 noise). Pipeline: 1 new field + 1 new enum + 2 new functions + 1 anaphora promotion + 1 planner short-circuit + 2 new template families. Cadence: patch ‚ÄĒ behavioural refinement on existing infrastructure, no new SemFrame field. **Stripe (9) ‚ÄĒ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.38.0 (HasQuantity ranking; subject synonym –į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ‚ÜĒ–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā; RelationKind population; remaining 6 parser tenses).

**v4.37.0 ‚ÄĒ ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –Ņ–Ķ?¬Ľ inversion-question routing ‚ÄĒ confirmation-seeking shape recognized.** First minor in v4.37+ semantic-IR arc. Closes v4.36.7 carry-forward. The ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –Ņ–Ķ?¬Ľ pattern ‚ÄĒ tag-question form like ¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ –ī“Ī—Ä—č—Ā –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –Ņ–Ķ?¬Ľ (¬ęisn't this correct?¬Ľ) ‚ÄĒ is **not** a denial; it's a confirmation-seeking inversion where speaker EXPECTS X to be true. Pre-fix, v4.33.5 negation routing misread these as denials. v4.37.0 detects via ¬ę–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ + question-particle co-occurrence and routes to dedicated family. **Before:** ¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ –ī“Ī—Ä—č—Ā –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –Ņ–Ķ?¬Ľ ‚Üí "–Ē“Ī—Ä—č—Ā –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –ī–Ķ–Ņ –į–Ļ—ā–į—Ā—č–∑ ‚ÄĒ –Ņ—Ė–ļ—Ė—Ä—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė —Ā—č–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ." (denial misread). **After:** "–ė”ô, –ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ —Ā–ĺ–Ľ–į–Ļ —ą—č“ď–į—Ä ‚ÄĒ –Ĺ–į“õ—ā—č –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–≥—Ė–ľ –∂–ĺ“õ." (inversion engagement). **(1)** New `Intent::Unknown.input_is_inversion_question: bool` field ‚ÄĒ fourth SemFrame-derived signal (after polarity, modality, evidence). **(2)** Conversation::turn detects ¬ę–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ (any inflected) + tag-question particle (–Ī–Ķ/–ľ–į/–ľ–Ķ/–Ņ–į/–Ņ–Ķ) co-occurrence. **(3)** Planner inversion routing ‚ÄĒ HIGHEST priority among Unknown-routing (before polarity). **(4)** Epistemic-override bypass mirrors prior pattern. **(5)** New template family `unknown.with_inversion_question` (7 templates) using hedging ¬ę–ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ / —ą—č“ď–į—Ä / —č“õ—ā–ł–ľ–į–Ľ¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ engages without confirmation or denial since adam lacks ground truth. **Battery case 18 reframed:** ¬ę–°–Ķ–Ĺ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ā—Ė“£ –Ī–Ķ?¬Ľ previously closed v4.34.0 as denial; v4.37.0 reroutes to inversion (semantically closer to intent). **v4.36.7 ‚ÄĒ EvidenceKind consumption on extraction side (Hearsay refuse) ‚ÄĒ Evidence cycle closed both sides.** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Adds third guard ‚ÄĒ Hearsay refusal ‚ÄĒ to all three migrated matchers, completing **triple-guard pattern**: negation + modality + evidentiality. **Principle:** if source sentence reports hearsay (¬ę–ź–Ī–į–Ļ –į“õ—č–Ĺ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ), promoting it to graph as `(–į–Ī–į–Ļ, IsA, –į“õ—č–Ĺ)` would lose evidential context and recompose hearsay as confirmed knowledge. Adam shouldn't fabricate certainty from reportative source. Refuse extraction. **Implementation:** triple-guard pattern in `copula_is_a`, `nominal_conjunction`, `locative_lives_in` ‚ÄĒ three sequential guards (negation + modality + Hearsay). All conservative ‚ÄĒ skip whole matcher on ANY signal. Zero cross-coupling. **Substrate-then-consume cycle: 3 of 4 SemFrame fields with FULLY closed cycles** ‚ÄĒ Polarity (v4.33.5+v4.34.5), Modality (v4.34.7+v4.35.0), Evidence (v4.36.0+**v4.36.7**); RelationKind remains placeholder. **Corpus impact:** RelatedTo 62 ‚Üí **56** (-6 from nominal_conjunction Hearsay guard rejecting source sentences with PastEvidential/PastReportative tense ‚ÄĒ speakers reporting hearsay about relation between two nouns); IsA 1472 unchanged; LivesIn 8 unchanged. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** unchanged; mean **191.5 ms / 176.1 MB** (-25 ms vs v4.36.6 ‚ÄĒ likely OS file-cache warmth, triple-guard adds minor hot-path cost); facts.json 1934 ‚Üí 1928; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **v4.36.x arc fully complete** ‚ÄĒ five releases (v4.36.0/.5/.6/.7) closed: third matcher migration + first dialog Hearsay consumption + PastReportative tense + ConverbPerfect/vowel-alternation/short-1sg FST coverage + Evidence extraction guard. **v4.36.6 ‚ÄĒ FST coverage: ¬ę–į–Ľ–į–ľ¬Ľ short-form 1sg + ¬ę–ĺ“õ–ł¬Ľ back-vowel converb (final v4.36.x FST gaps closed).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Limited to 1sg (other persons don't contract in standard Kazakh). **Live verification:** ¬ę–ě“õ–ł¬Ľ / ¬ę–ě“õ–ł–ī—č¬Ľ now parse (was: no parse); ¬ę–ź–Ľ–į–ľ¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ď–į—Ä–į–ľ¬Ľ now parse with `tense=Present person=First`; ¬ę–Ė–į–∑–į –į–Ľ–į–ľ¬Ľ ‚Üí "–Ė–į“õ—Ā—č –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ, —Ā—Ė–∑–ī—Ė“£ –ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–≥—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ľ." (full ability detection works on short form); long forms ¬ę–į–Ľ–į–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ unchanged. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent**; mean **216.1 ms / 177.1 MB** (+21 ms vs v4.36.5 ‚ÄĒ real perf cost from vowel-alternation check + short-form synth+compare per matching feature combo; honest trade for closing two architectural gaps); facts 1934 unchanged; all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **v4.36.x arc complete** ‚ÄĒ three releases (v4.36.0 ‚Üí v4.36.5 ‚Üí v4.36.6) closed all v4.36+ FST coverage and consumption work. **v4.36.5 ‚ÄĒ FST coverage: ConverbPerfect + PastReportative (¬ę–∂–į–∑—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ī–ĺ–Ľ—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ now route to Hearsay).** Patch in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Closes the v4.36.0 honest-gap carry-forward ‚ÄĒ the ¬ę-{Y}–Ņ(—ā—č)¬Ľ reportative form, which is the natural Kazakh hearsay form most commonly produced in user dialog, previously didn't parse at all. **Before:** ¬ę–Ė–į–∑—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ ‚Üí "–Ę“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ī–Ķ–ī—Ė–ľ." **After:** "–°—Ė–∑–≥–Ķ –į–Ļ—ā—č–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ —Ā–ł—Ź“õ—ā—č –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ –Ĺ–į“õ—ā—č –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–≥—Ė–ľ –∂–ĺ“õ." **(1)** New `Tense::PastReportative` variant, distinct from `PastEvidential` (both encode hearsay but differ structurally: PastEvidential = `-“ď–į–Ĺ/-–≥–Ķ–Ĺ` participle base + person endings; PastReportative = `-{Y}–Ņ` perfect-converb base + invariant `-—ā—č` particle, no person ending). **(2)** New synth template `VERB_REPORTATIVE_PAST` + match arm in `synthesise_verb`. **(3)** SemFrame maps `PastReportative ‚Üí Hearsay` alongside existing `PastEvidential ‚Üí Hearsay`. **(4)** Parser tenses += `ConverbPerfect, PastReportative` (alongside v4.32.5's ConverbImperfect) ‚ÄĒ closes ConverbPerfect bare form parsing as bonus (¬ę–∂–į–∑—č–Ņ¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė–Ņ¬Ľ / ¬ę–ĺ“õ—č–Ņ¬Ľ now parse). **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged; real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 %** coherent unchanged; mean **194.6 ms / 177.1 MB** (-127 ms vs v4.36.0 ‚ÄĒ most likely OS file-cache warmth, not true perf improvement; adding 2 tenses costs ~30 % more parse work per verb); facts.json 1935 ‚Üí 1934 (-1 RelatedTo from new ConverbPerfect parse triggering guard); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ‚úď; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ‚úď; rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď; foundation passes. **Live verification:** ¬ę–Ė–į–∑—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ď–ĺ–Ľ—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ / ¬ę–ź–Ī–į–Ļ –∂–į–∑—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ all hearsay-aware; ¬ę–Ė–į–∑—č–Ņ¬Ľ (bare ConverbPerfect) now parses; controls (¬ę–Ė–į–∑“ď–į–Ĺ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ PastEvidential / ¬ę–Ė–į–∑–ī—č¬Ľ PastDefinite / ¬ę–ź–Ī–į–Ļ –∂–į–∑–ī—č¬Ľ) unchanged. **Honest re-scope:** v4.36.5 was originally promised to also close ¬ę–į–Ľ–į–ľ¬Ľ (short-form 1sg) + ¬ę–ĺ“õ–ł¬Ľ (back-vowel converb). Those turn out to need separate FST architecture work ‚ÄĒ ¬ę–į–Ľ–į–ľ¬Ľ needs short-form personal-ending alternates (invasive); ¬ę–ĺ“õ–ł¬Ľ needs stem-alternation paradigm matcher (vowel-final back-vowel verbs break prefix-match). Both deferred to v4.36.6+. Pipeline: 1 new Tense variant + 1 synth template + 1 match arm + 1 SemFrame evidence mapping line + 2 parser enumeration entries + facts regen. **v4.36.0 ‚ÄĒ Third matcher migration + first EvidenceKind consumption (Hearsay hedging).** First minor in v4.36+ semantic-IR arc. Two architectural completions in one release: (a) `locative_lives_in` joins `copula_is_a` (v4.34.5) and `nominal_conjunction` (v4.35.0) as third extract_facts matcher migrated to consume `&[SemFrame]`, with same dual-guard pattern (negation + modality refusal); (b) **first EvidenceKind consumption** ‚ÄĒ Hearsay-marked utterances now route to a respectful hedging template family. Third SemFrame field to influence user-facing answer text after Polarity (v4.33.5) and Modality (v4.34.7). **(1)** `locative_lives_in` migrated: + `sem_frames`, dual guards. **(2)** New `Intent::Unknown.input_evidence: Option<EvidenceKind>` field. **(3)** Conversation::turn populates from any sem_frame's evidence (independent of noun_hint, like modality). **(4)** Planner Hearsay routing AFTER polarity + modality (lower priority ‚ÄĒ when those fire, more salient signal wins): `if matches!(input_evidence, Some(Hearsay)) ‚Üí "unknown.with_hearsay_hedge"`. **(5)** Epistemic-override bypass for Hearsay (mirrors v4.34.0/v4.34.7). **(6)** New template family with 7 templates: ¬ę–°—Ė–∑–≥–Ķ –į–Ļ—ā—č–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ —Ā–ł—Ź“õ—ā—č –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ –Ĺ–į“õ—ā—č –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–≥—Ė–ľ –∂–ĺ“õ¬Ľ, ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –Ķ—Ā—ā—Ė–≥–Ķ–Ĺ —Ā”©–∑ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—Ā–į –ļ–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ, –Ī—Ė—Ä–į“õ –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ —ā–Ķ–ļ—Ā–Ķ—Ä–Ķ –į–Ľ–ľ–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ. **Live:** ¬ę–Ė–į–∑“ď–į–Ĺ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ ‚Üí trace shows `–∂–į–∑/Verb tense=PastEvidential evid=Hearsay`, response: "–°—Ė–∑–≥–Ķ –į–Ļ—ā—č–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ —Ā–ł—Ź“õ—ā—č –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ –Ĺ–į“õ—ā—č –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–≥—Ė–ľ –∂–ĺ“õ" ‚úď; ¬ę–ź–Ī–į–Ļ –∂–į–∑–ī—č¬Ľ (PastDefinite control) ‚Üí unchanged ‚úď. **Substrate-then-consume cycle status (3 of 4 fields with closed dialog cycles):** Polarity (v4.33.5+v4.34.5), Modality (v4.34.7+v4.35.0), Evidence (**v4.36.0** dialog only ‚ÄĒ extraction side TBD); RelationKind still placeholder. **Verification:** Workspace **865 passing** unchanged (8 test-site Intent::Unknown patches added `input_evidence: None`); real-world **26-query battery 26/26 = 100 % coherent** unchanged; mean **321.9 ms / 175.8 MB** (+1.6 ms vs v4.35.5, within noise); facts.json 1935 unchanged (locative_lives_in guard didn't reject current LivesIn facts); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** ¬ę-{Y}–Ņ(—ā—č)¬Ľ reportative forms (¬ę–∂–į–∑—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ī–ĺ–Ľ—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ) do NOT currently parse ‚ÄĒ FST treats Tense::PastEvidential as the ¬ę–∂–į–∑“ď–į–Ĺ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ-style construction. Closing the ¬ę-—č–Ņ—ā—č¬Ľ path is v4.36.5+ FST coverage work. **v4.35.5 ‚ÄĒ Modal-without-noun: battery case 21 ¬ę–Ė–į–∑–į –į–Ľ–į–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ closes.** Patch in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. **v4.35.0 ‚ÄĒ Second extract_facts matcher migration + modality guard on extraction side.** First minor in v4.35+ semantic-IR arc. **v4.33.0 ‚ÄĒ Sentence-level negation: ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ ‚Üí Polarity::Negated on prior noun.** First minor in v4.33+ semantic-feature population arc. Closes the noun-polarity gap left by v4.31.0 ‚ÄĒ `Polarity` was unified across nouns and verbs but only auto-derived from `VerbFeatures.negation` (verb-level). v4.33.0 adds sentence-level detection: when a noun-class frame is followed by ¬ę–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ (¬ęnot¬Ľ) particle, the noun's polarity flips to `Negated`. The Kazakh polarity story is now architecturally complete for non-inflected patterns. **(1)** `populate_sentential_negation(&mut [SemFrame])` ‚ÄĒ single linear scan; for each `frame[i].root == "–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā"`, mark `frame[i-1].polarity = Negated` if predecessor is noun-like (Noun / Adjective / Pronoun / Numeral). Verb frames skipped (their negation comes from `VerbFeatures.negation`, FST-level). **(2)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER ability detection. Live: ¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ —ą—č–Ĺ–ī—č“õ –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ ‚Üí `[1] —ą—č–Ĺ–ī—č“õ/Noun polarity=Negated`; ¬ę–ě–Ľ “Ī–∑—č–Ĺ –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ ‚Üí `[1] “Ī–∑—č–Ĺ/Adjective polarity=Negated`. Negation attaches to immediate predecessor (the actual content head), not to leading pronoun. **(3) Known FST gap (carry-forward to v4.34+):** inflected forms ¬ę–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—Ė–Ĺ / –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ā—Ė“£ / –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—Ė–∑ / –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ā—Ė–∑¬Ľ do NOT parse ‚ÄĒ `parser::analyse` dispatches `particle` POS through catch-all branch (bare-only). ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ X –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—Ė–Ĺ¬Ľ loses the inflected token; detection blocked until parser's particle dispatch is extended to enumerate predicate copulas. Documented as v4.34+ prerequisite. **Verification:** Workspace **854 ‚Üí 860 passing** (+6 negation tests: bare-noun, leading-pronoun-attachment, verb-skip, no-match negative, position-zero skipped, idempotence); real-world **24-query battery 23/24 = 95.8 %** coherent (no regression vs v4.32.5; case 21 still honest "–Ę“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ī–Ķ–ī—Ė–ľ" on declarative ability); **modal-detect 4/4**, **neg-detect 2/2**; mean **322.5 ms / 177.0 MB** RSS (-2.9 ms vs v4.32.5, within noise ‚ÄĒ negation detection adds zero measurable cost); all holdouts unchanged; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** Polarity::Negated populated on noun frames in canonical pattern but **not yet consumed** by response generator ‚ÄĒ text unchanged. Polarity-aware response generation is v4.33.5+ work. The polarity story is now architecturally complete: verbs derive from FST-level `VerbFeatures.negation`; nouns/adjectives derive from sentential ¬ę–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ (this release). Pipeline: 1 new function (~40 lines) + 1 re-export + 1 turn_with_trace line + 6 unit tests + battery 22‚Üí24 + facts version sync. Cadence: minor ‚ÄĒ closes meaningful gap that v4.31.0 deliberately left for a future release. **Stripe (9) ‚ÄĒ semantic IR layer continues.** Next: v4.33.5 (first consumption of SemFrame fields ‚ÄĒ template branching on Polarity + Modality); v4.34.0 (parser particle-copula extension + first extract_facts pattern matcher migration to `&[SemFrame]`); v4.35+ (remaining 8 parser tenses; battery edge case 18 ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā –Ņ–Ķ?¬Ľ question form).

**v4.32.5 ‚ÄĒ Ability `-–į –į–Ľ-` detection + parser tense expansion (ConverbImperfect).** Patch in v4.32+ semantic-feature population arc ‚ÄĒ closes the third member of the Kazakh modality triad. Honest scope-creep: ability detection required a prerequisite parser fix (FST verb analyser only enumerated 4 of 13 defined tenses, blocking converb forms like ¬ę–∂–į–∑–į¬Ľ). Fixing both together is the matched architectural pair. **(1)** `parser::try_verb_analyses` tense enumeration += `ConverbImperfect`. Cost: ~25 % more parse time per verb token (5 instead of 4 tenses). Conservative ‚ÄĒ adds only the one tense ability detection needs. Other 8 missing tenses (ConverbPerfect, 3 participles, FutureIntentional, FuturePossible, Conditional, Imperative) deferred to releases that need them. **(2)** `populate_ability_modality(&mut [SemFrame])` with **dual-signal check**: signal (a) current frame's `root == "–į–Ľ"` AND `pos == Verb`; signal (b) preceding frame's `tense == Some(ConverbImperfect)`. Both required ‚ÄĒ eliminates false positive on ¬ę–ö—Ė—ā–į–Ņ—ā—č –į–Ľ–ī—č–ľ¬Ľ ("I took the book") where `–į–Ľ` is just the regular transitive verb. **(3)** Wired into `turn_with_trace` AFTER `populate_periphrastic_modality`; first-detection-wins. Live: ¬ę–Ė–į–∑–į –į–Ľ–į–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ ‚Üí `[0] –∂–į–∑/Verb tense=ConverbImperfect mod=Ability`. **Verification:** Workspace **847 ‚Üí 854 passing** (+7 ability tests: canonical, negated-aux, no-false-positive-noun, no-false-positive-finite, single-frame, preset-preservation, idempotence); real-world **22-query battery 21/22 = 95.5 % coherent** (1 honest "–Ę“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ī–Ķ–ī—Ė–ľ" on declarative ability ‚ÄĒ no template for "user declares they can do X", v4.x intent gap not a regression); **modal-detect 4/4 = 100 %** in --trace (Necessity + Possibility + Ability √ó2); mean **325.4 ms / 176.2 MB RSS** (+1.9 ms vs v4.32.0 ‚ÄĒ within noise, tracks parser tense expansion). Live highlight: ¬ę–°”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ ‚Üí ability detected on —Ā”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ + intent=AskAboutSystem(GenericCapability) + honest "–Ė–ĺ“õ, –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ ”ô—Ä–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—ā—ā—Ė ”©–∑—Ė–ľ –ĺ—Ä—č–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –į–Ľ–ľ–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ" ‚ÄĒ three layers working together. **Honest framing:** Kazakh modality triad (Necessity / Possibility / Ability) now **fully populated** in SemFrame as auto-derivations on the lexical predicate; any v4.33+ consumer can read these fields without re-deriving. Modality still **not consumed** by response generator ‚ÄĒ template branching is v4.33+. Pipeline: 1 line in parser tenses + 1 new ~30-line function + 1 re-export + 1 turn_with_trace line + 7 unit tests + battery extended 20‚Üí22 + facts version sync. **v4.32.0 ‚ÄĒ Modality population from periphrastic auxiliaries (–ļ–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ / —ā–ł—Ė—Ā / –ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ).** First minor in v4.32+ semantic-feature population arc, second SemFrame consumer migration. First-detection-wins discipline (won't overwrite preset modality). **(2)** Wired into `Conversation::turn_with_trace` after sem_frames construction; visible live in `--trace`: ¬ę–Ė–į–∑—É –ļ–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ¬Ľ ‚Üí `[0] –∂–į–∑—É/Noun mod=Necessity`. **(3)** Conservative on ability `-–į –į–Ľ-` (auxiliary `–į–Ľ` is also a transitive verb meaning "take/get" ‚ÄĒ naive surface detection would mis-mark genuine "X took Y" as ability-modal; deferred to v4.32.5+ with proper converb + person-marked-–į–Ľ check). **Verification:** Workspace **839 ‚Üí 847 passing** (+8 modality tests: kerek/tiis/mumkin detection, no-match negative, single-frame noop, sentence-initial-modal-skipped, idempotence, preset-preservation); real-world **20-query battery 20/20 = 100 % coherent**, modal-detect 2/2 in --trace; mean **323.5 ms / 175.9 MB RSS** (within noise vs v4.31.5 ‚ÄĒ modality detection adds zero measurable cost); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ‚úď; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ‚úď; rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď; foundation passes. **Honest framing:** `modality` is now populated but **not consumed** ‚ÄĒ for ¬ę–ö—Ė—ā–į–Ņ –ĺ“õ—É –ļ–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ¬Ľ the response is the same general fact about –ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ. Trace shows `mod=Necessity` correctly; downstream template branching is v4.33+ work. **v4.31.0 ‚ÄĒ Morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame) substrate.** First minor in v4.31+ semantic-IR arc ‚ÄĒ the architectural step the 2026-05-02 Codex consultation correctly identified as next. Converts agglutination from a tokenizer-improvement into the **internal logic of the system** by introducing a single typed semantic frame that carries each word's full morphological + logical features through the pipeline downstream of FST. v4.31.0 ships **substrate only** ‚ÄĒ type + lossless conversion + 8 unit tests. No consumers wired (substrate-first pattern, mirror of v4.0.37 ‚Üí v4.0.38). **(1)** New `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/sem_frame.rs` (~520 lines + 8 tests). Defines `SemFrame { root, pos, case, number, possessive, predicate, derivation, tense, person, voice, polarity, polite, modality, evidence, relation }` plus closed enums `PosTag` / `Polarity` / `Modality` / `EvidenceKind` / `RelationKind`. **(2)** `SemFrame::from_analysis(&Analysis)` + `impl From<&Analysis>` ‚ÄĒ lossless: every NounFeatures / VerbFeatures field flows through. Auto-derives `polarity = Negated` when `VerbFeatures.negation == true`; `evidence = Some(Hearsay)` when `Tense::PastEvidential`; nouns default `Affirmative` polarity (sentence-level ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ is v4.32+). `Modality` and `RelationKind` are placeholder slots for v4.32+ work ‚ÄĒ always `None` in v4.31.0. **(3)** Re-exports in lib.rs: `SemFrame`, `PosTag`, `Polarity`, `Modality`, `EvidenceKind`, `RelationKind` ‚ÄĒ single import for downstream crates. **Verification:** Workspace **831 ‚Üí 839 passing** (+8 SemFrame tests: noun roundtrip, verb roundtrip, negation‚ÜíNegated, PastEvidential‚ÜíHearsay, POS projection covers all 5 classes + Function fallback, polite verb preserved, trait equivalence, determinism); live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ‚úď; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ‚úď; rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď; foundation passes. **Runtime behaviour change: zero.** v4.31.0 adds the type but wires zero consumers ‚ÄĒ bit-for-bit identical to v4.30.5. **What this is NOT:** not a runtime change (consumer migration starts v4.31.5); not a deletion of Analysis (SemFrame is a higher-level wrapping); not a neural component. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 mod registration + 6 re-exports + facts version sync. Cadence: minor ‚ÄĒ first release of a new architectural primitive that will flow through every downstream consumer over the v4.31.x arc. **Stripe (9) ‚ÄĒ semantic IR layer opens.** Next: **v4.31.5** (first consumer ‚ÄĒ extend `--trace` to emit SemFrame per parsed token, OR migrate one extract_facts matcher); **v4.32.0** (populate modality from periphrastic constructions; populate relation from pattern matchers); **v4.33.0+** (sentence-level ¬ęX –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā¬Ľ detection; SemFrame as canonical SearchGraph query input).

**v4.30.5 ‚ÄĒ Precision sweep: DoesTo extraction disabled; +engineering thesis in README; +unified KPI.** Patch in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc, prompted by 2026-05-02 strategic consultation. **(1)** `patterns::agent_verb` (DoesTo extractor) DISABLED in production pipeline. Audit found 125 / 196 = **64 % of corpus-extracted relations** came from this single matcher (`X Y-–Ĺ—Ė V-–Ľ–į–Ļ–ī—č`); review confirmed pairs were surface verbal-phrase co-occurrences, not stable relations: ¬ę–∂–į“£–Ī—č—Ä does_to –∂–Ķ—Ä¬Ľ, ¬ę–ļ—Ā—Ä–ĺ does_to –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā¬Ľ, ¬ę—Ä–Ķ—ā does_to –Ķ–Ľ¬Ľ. Function and its 4 unit tests preserved for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable. **Result:** 196 ‚Üí 71 Grammar facts (-64 %); HumanApproved share rises **90.5 % ‚Üí 96.3 %** of committed graph. **(2)** Engineering thesis subsection added to README ‚ÄĒ makes the project's claim explicit and provable: agglutinative morphology gives a clean algebra of meaning (root + typed suffix operators), composition is rule-bound, that's what we build on. Same engineering style applies to Turkish/Kyrgyz/Tatar/Uzbek without claims of universal grammar or historical primacy. **(3)** Unified KPI in `docs/performance.md`: `latency_ms_per_correct_answer = p50_turn_latency_ms / holdout_pass_rate` folds speed + correctness into one comparable number; pass-rate denominator is full workspace test count, so adding 50 tests but dropping one has a measurably worse cost-per-correct even at unchanged latency. v4.30.5 baseline: **1.07 ms / correct answer**. **Verification:** Workspace **831 passing** unchanged; facts.json 2059 ‚Üí 1934 (exact -125 DoesTo drop); HumanApproved 90.5 % ‚Üí 96.3 %; live_holdout_2026_05_02 5/5 ‚úď; live_holdout_2026_05_01 32/32 ‚úď; rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď; foundation validation passes. **What this is NOT:** not a fix for the bigger precision risk at 10k+-fact auto-extraction scale (v4.31+ topic if we ramp); not a deletion of `agent_verb` (kept for future semantic-class-filtered re-enable); not the morphemic-logical IR work ‚ÄĒ that's v4.31.0. Pipeline: 1 line commented + extensive rationale + 1 README subsection + 1 performance.md section + facts regen. Cadence: patch ‚ÄĒ gigienic correction without architectural change. **Stripe (8) ‚ÄĒ multi-turn coherence layer continues.** Next: **v4.31.0 ‚ÄĒ morphemic-logical IR (SemFrame)**, the architectural step Codex correctly identified.

**v4.30.0 ‚ÄĒ Coreference layer + Rust extraction patches: live REPL 2026-05-02 regressions closed.** First minor in v4.30+ dialog-coherence arc. A 2026-05-02 live REPL session surfaced three failures: (1) ¬ęRust –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ extracted topic ¬ę—ā—Ė–Ľ¬Ľ instead of ¬ęRust¬Ľ; (2) ¬ę–†–į—Ā—ā¬Ľ (Cyrillic) had no alias; (3) follow-up ¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī–Ķ–≥—Ė –ļ—Ė–Ľ—ā —Ā”©–∑–ī–Ķ—Ä?¬Ľ couldn't resolve `–Ī“Ī–Ľ —ā—Ė–Ľ` to the prior Rust topic ‚ÄĒ v4.13.0 handled bare-pronoun anaphors but not adnominal demonstratives. v4.30.0 closes all three. **(1)** New `latin_with_generic_head_marker` matches ¬ę{LATIN_TECH_SUBJECT} (–Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É|–Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≥—Ä–į–ľ–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É)? {generic head} {topic marker}¬Ľ and returns the Latin head directly ‚ÄĒ short-circuits the multiword scanner (¬ę–Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė¬Ľ) and topic_marker_hint (¬ę—ā—Ė–Ľ¬Ľ) which both extracted the wrong constituent. 9 generic heads √ó 4 markers √ó 0‚Äď1 qualifier. **(2)** New `input_contains_adnominal_demonstrative` recognises ¬ę{–Ī“Ī–Ľ/–ĺ—Ā—č/—Ā–ĺ–Ľ} + {generic head}¬Ľ as a coreference signal; `input_contains_discourse_anaphor` now fires for both bare pronouns (v4.13.0) AND adnominal demonstratives (v4.30.0). The downstream `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()` path resolves both signals identically. **(3)** programming_rust.jsonl += rust_180 (`–†–į—Ā—ā` Cyrillic alias) + rust_181 (programming-language list-summary). **(4)** MULTIWORD_ENTITIES += ¬ęrust —ā—Ė–∑—Ė–ľ—Ė¬Ľ. **(5)** New `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_02.json` (5 cases) + dedicated test rig with **multi-turn `context_turns` support** ‚ÄĒ first multi-turn case in the holdout suite (demonstrative-coreference case requires prior Rust establishment). **Verification:** Workspace tests **830 ‚Üí 831 passing** (+1 holdout); live_holdout_2026_05_02 **5/5 = 100 %**; live_holdout_2026_05_01 **32/32 ‚úď**; rust_holdout **41/41 ‚úď**; foundation validation passes. **What's NOT solved (carry-forwards):** plural-form multiword (¬ę“ö–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė–Ĺ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ still falls through ‚ÄĒ needs morpho-aware multiword scanning or list-intent trigger on ¬ę“õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ ... –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑¬Ľ) ‚Üí v4.30.5+; functional/compositional queries (¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī–Ķ —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź–Ĺ—č “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –∂–į–∑–į–ľ—č–∑?¬Ľ) ‚ÄĒ coreference resolves but no curated Rust+function entry ‚Üí v4.31+ compositional-reasoning track; physics domain (zero curated entries) ‚Üí v4.30.5+. **Honest framing:** this release closes the three failures the user surfaced and adds the first-ever multi-turn coreference path (bare pronouns + adnominal demonstratives now both flow through `dialog_context.resolve_anaphor()`). Subjective "context retention" should improve on follow-up questions; subjective "intelligence" doesn't improve because the system still does retrieval+ranking, not synthesis ‚ÄĒ that gap is on v4.31+. Pipeline: 1 recogniser + 1 coreference detector + 1 MULTIWORD + 2 world_core + 1 holdout JSON + 1 test rig + facts regen. **v4.29.5 ‚ÄĒ Track A Phase 2: RootAffinity wired into runtime SearchGraph reranking.** Phase 2 of v4.29.0's Track A ‚ÄĒ runtime integration of the PMI matrix shipped as a deferred-wiring artifact. **(1)** New `Conversation::with_root_affinity(affinity)` builder mirroring v4.15.5's `with_suffix_priors`; optional, when not attached ranking is bit-for-bit identical to v4.29.0. **(2)** `ToolContext.root_affinity: Option<&RootAffinity>` field threaded through every `Conversation::turn` so each `SearchGraph` dispatch sees the matrix. **(3)** Affinity tier inserted at the **deepest semantic depth** ‚ÄĒ after `length`, before lexicographic. Initial draft placed it between `domain_match` and `length`, but the `world_core_water` holdout regression revealed that PMI cultural co-occurrence (`—Ā—É ‚ÜĒ —Ā—É—Ā—č–Ĺ` in food-context corpus) can outrank length, which is a strong "informativeness" signal. The deepest placement preserves all v4.29.0 ranking outcomes while still firing on truly equivalent candidates ‚ÄĒ exactly the use case PMI was trained for. **(4)** Live `adam_chat` startup wiring loads `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` if present; logs `"adam-chat: root affinity ‚ÄĒ {n_roots} roots, {n_pairs} pairs over {n_samples} training samples"`. Missing file or schema mismatch is non-fatal. **(5)** Holdout test rigs (`live_holdout`, `rust_holdout`) load the matrix when present so the regression suite runs in production-shape configuration. **Ranking ladder post-v4.29.5:** `list_intent_rank ‚Üí overlap ‚Üí predicate_priority ‚Üí domain_match ‚Üí length DESC ‚Üí root_affinity DESC ‚Üź NEW ‚Üí lexicographic ASC`. **Verification:** Workspace tests **829 ‚Üí 830 passing** (+1 new `search_graph_root_affinity_breaks_length_tie` proves the tier flips an alphabetically-losing candidate when PMI is decisive); live_holdout 32/32 ‚úď with affinity ON; rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď with affinity ON; **9-query live ON-vs-OFF probe all bit-identical** (the tier is conservative on current world_core where length usually disambiguates ‚ÄĒ production benefits accumulate as curated graph grows length-tied candidates). **Honest limitation:** the matrix was trained over a corpus dominated by general/news/textbook contexts; specialty-domain PMI (chemistry, medicine, programming) is sparse ‚ÄĒ bridging this is on the v4.30+ roadmap. Pipeline: 1 builder + 1 ToolContext field + 1 ranking tier + 1 unit test + adam_chat load wiring + 2 holdout test load wirings + facts/derived_facts version sync. Cadence: patch ‚ÄĒ runtime integration of an already-shipped artifact, conservative tier placement. **Stripe (7) ‚ÄĒ Track A discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.30.0 (per-domain PMI matrices + cross-turn topic carry via previous_grounded_fact + Result-—ā—č Accusative-with-dash tokenizer fix).

**v4.29.0 ‚ÄĒ Track A discourse-level prior: RootAffinity (PMI matrix) ‚ÄĒ 834k pairs across 10 523 roots.** First minor in v4.29+ Track A discourse-level statistical layer. v4.15 ‚Üí v4.20 built SuffixPriors for chain-level morphology disambiguation. v4.28.5 expanded corpus 5.77M ‚Üí 8.85M tokens. v4.29.0 ships **first cross-word semantic signal**: sparse PMI matrix over root pairs that co-occur in same sample. **Phase 1 only ‚ÄĒ artifact + type + training binary**; runtime integration deferred to v4.29.5. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/root_affinity.rs` (~250 lines + 5 unit tests). `RootAffinity { version, trained_on_samples, min_pair_count, root_log_prob, pair_pmi }` ‚ÄĒ sparse map indexed `outer_root ‚Üí inner_root ‚Üí PMI` with lex-smaller-first key normalization. **(2)** Why PMI not raw count: raw co-occurrence dominated by ubiquitous roots (–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ/–ĺ–Ľ/–Ī—Ė—Ä) ‚ÄĒ produce no signal. PMI normalizes by marginals: `log(P(a,b) / (P(a)¬∑P(b)))`. Filter `MIN_PAIR_COUNT = 5` suppresses small-sample noise. **(3)** New training binary `train_root_affinity.rs` ‚ÄĒ three-pass algorithm (collect samples ‚Üí FST-analyse unique tokens ‚Üí walk samples accumulating single+pair counts). Output: `data/retrieval/root_affinity.json` byte-stable sorted. **Trained on v4.28.5 corpus:** 1,076,271 samples / 10,523 roots / 3,389,957 pairs pre-filter / **834,053 pairs post-filter** (24.6% survival) / 6,662 outer roots / 26 MB JSON / ~1.5 min training time. **Sample affinities:** –∂–į—Ā—É—ą–į‚ÜĒ—Ź–ī—Ä–ĺ=4.29, –į—ā–ĺ–ľ‚ÜĒ—Ź–ī—Ä–ĺ=4.28, –Ī–į–Ľ–į‚ÜĒ–į–Ĺ–į=2.11, —ā–į—É‚ÜĒ–ļ”©–Ľ=2.09, –ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ‚ÜĒ—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ=1.03, –∂–Ķ—Ä‚ÜĒ–ļ“Į–Ĺ=0.50, rust‚ÜĒcargo=0.0 (Latin not in Kazakh lexicon ‚Üí handled separately). **Verification:** Workspace tests **824 ‚Üí 829 passing** (+5 root_affinity unit tests); rust_holdout 41/41 ‚úď; live_holdout 32/32 ‚úď; parse-disambig 23/23 ‚úď; 80-q battery 79/80 (zero behavior change since Phase 1). **What v4.29.5 will enable:** `Conversation::with_root_affinity(...)` builder mirroring `with_suffix_priors`; `current_topic_root` in ToolContext; affinity tiebreaker in `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` ranking ladder. Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 new artifact + facts version sync. Cadence: minor ‚ÄĒ first artifact in new prior axis (chain ‚Üí root pair). Architectural addition, zero runtime behavior change. **Stripe (7) ‚ÄĒ Track A corpus expansion ‚Üí discourse-prior layer.** Next: v4.29.5 (runtime integration of RootAffinity into reranking).

**v4.25.0 ‚ÄĒ R5 degree-based hub filter (Codex actionable #5): ‚ąí75.5 % derived facts, holdout still 100 %.** First minor in v4.25+ engineering-hygiene arc. Closes 5th Codex review actionable. Pre-fix, **22931/25006 = 91.7 %** of derived facts came from a single rule (`R5_shared_is_a_target`: A IsA X ‚ąß B IsA X ‚üĻ RelatedTo(A, B)) ‚ÄĒ Codex identified this as source of tangential-answer risk. The v4.0.23 named-list filter only caught 5 categorical-abstract hubs (–∑–į—ā/–Ī–Ķ–Ľ–≥—Ė/”ô—Ä–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—ā/“õ“Ī–Ī—č–Ľ—č—Ā/–į–ī–į–ľ); the long tail of mid-degree hubs (10‚Äď50 incoming IsA each) generated cartesian-product RelatedTo pairs (ūĚĎĎ¬∑(ūĚĎĎ‚ąí1)/2) that crowded the derivation pool without dialog-relevant value. **(1)** New `MAX_R5_HUB_DEGREE = 8` constant in `crates/adam-reasoning/src/reasoner.rs`. Any hub with > 8 incoming IsA edges is skipped wholesale. Structural complement to the named filter ‚ÄĒ runs before the cartesian-product loop. **(2)** Threshold tuned empirically against the v4.24.5 live holdout: chosen so all `unknown.with_derived_chain` fixtures continue to produce a derivation (no ¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā-¬Ľ template variant goes red) and live_holdout stays at 100 %, while reduction is large enough to materially change pool composition. **Impact:** Total derived facts **25 006 ‚Üí 6 137 (‚ąí18 869, ‚ąí75.5 %)**; R5 derivations **22 931 ‚Üí 1 159 (‚ąí95.0 %)**; R5 share **91.7 % ‚Üí 18.9 %**; `derived_facts.json` ~14 MB ‚Üí ~3.5 MB. **Verification:** Workspace tests **823 ‚Üí 823 passing**; live holdout **32/32 = 100.0 %**; parse-disambig eval still **23/23 = 100 %**. The reduction is entirely tangential bloat that no existing test actually consumed. **Why this matters beyond the metric:** with 22 931 R5 derivations dominating the candidate pool, retrieval ranking had a structural bias toward surfacing RelatedTo chains over curated direct facts. v4.25.0 shrinks the pool the ranker sees from ~25 K ‚Üí ~6 K candidates. Sets up domain-aware scoring (the second half of Codex's recommendation) to be a smaller follow-up patch. Pipeline: 1 constant + 1 skip branch (~30-line addition) + artifact regeneration. No schema diff, no API change, no template change. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (5) ‚ÄĒ humanness through real-dialog testing ‚ÄĒ derivation hygiene layer.** Codex queue is now down to **one item**: v4.25.5 (README badge automation).

**v4.24.5 ‚ÄĒ live holdout eval (Codex actionable #4): blind substring-based regression baseline.** Patch in v4.24+ engineering-hygiene arc. Closes 4th Codex review actionable: every existing eval suite is curated regression ‚ÄĒ hand-tuned over ~20 releases, definitionally not blind. v4.24.5 adds the missing signal: a captured set of unedited queries from the 2026-05-01 live battery, run with no template tuning to make any specific case pass, with substring presence/absence rules instead of exact matches so template variants are tolerated. **(1)** New `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_01.json` ‚ÄĒ 32 unedited queries across 12 categories (identity / world_core_science / world_core_geo / world_core_culture / world_core_history / math / temporal_no_data / compositional_function / honest_unknown / willingness / acknowledgment / profile_capture). Schema: `any_substring` (pass if any present) + `none_substring` (pass if none present), AND-combined. **Capture rule:** never edit a captured set after it lands; future captures (`live_holdout_YYYYMMDD.json`) extend coverage as separate files. **(2)** New `crates/adam-dialog/tests/live_holdout.rs` integration test ‚ÄĒ production-shaped `Conversation` setup (lexicon + templates + morpheme index + reasoning + priors őĪ=0.3 + domain index), reports overall + per-category pass rate, asserts ‚Č• 70 % baseline floor. **Baseline (v4.24.5):** **32/32 = 100.0 %** first-run pass rate across all 12 categories. Validates that v4.22.5 ‚Üí v4.23.5 honest-fallback work successfully addressed every concrete failure from the 2026-05-01 session, not just the 4 directly-patched cases. Holdout doesn't *prove* quality is good ‚ÄĒ it *records* current behaviour so future regressions are visible; pass rate may legitimately drop on the next capture and gate at 70 % leaves headroom. **Known limitations:** substring matching is shallow (paraphrase drift may fail; confident-wrong assertions may pass); single-turn only (multi-turn lives in `repl_replay`); no latency/cost gate. Future captures can layer `expected_kind` semantic checks. Pipeline: 1 new data file (32 cases) + 1 new test (~210 lines). No production changes, no schema diffs. **v4.22.0 ‚ÄĒ runtime integration of chain_tiebreak_root: priors+root infrastructure now reaches live dialog.** First minor in v4.22+ runtime-integration arc. v4.19.0 ‚Üí v4.21.5 built the parse-disambiguation eval framework, surfaced the chain-collision blind spot, added root-level priors with closed-class boost, and shipped the FST pronoun-paradigm matcher ‚ÄĒ closing the eval at 100 % across 23 cases. **But that 100 % only applied inside the eval binary.** The actual dialog runtime (`parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`) was still using chain-only smoothed scoring without the root tiebreak. v4.22.0 closes the loop. **(1)** Runtime comparator in `parse_input_inner` extended ‚ÄĒ chain-prior re-rank gains a root-tiebreaker tier (`chain_diff < EPSILON` ‚Üí `score_root(root)` decides). Same logic as the eval's `pick_chain_with_root_tiebreak` from v4.20.0; `EPSILON = 1e-4` matches eval. **(2)** Strictly additive on the no-priors path ‚ÄĒ when `priors: None` is passed, the comparator block is skipped entirely; `parse_input` returns the v3.2.0 deterministic order bit-for-bit. **(3)** Three new runtime regression tests in `runtime_priors_tests` ‚ÄĒ load real frozen artifact + lexicon and assert production parse picks gold pronoun root for –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į ‚Üí –ĺ–Ľ, –ľ–į“ď–į–Ĺ ‚Üí –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ, —Ā–į“ď–į–Ĺ ‚Üí —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ. Plus a no-priors equivalence test. **What does NOT change:** 8 eval strategies in eval_parse_disambiguation unchanged (`chain_tiebreak_root` still 23/23 = 100 %, chain-only still 21/23 = 91.3 %); all non-pronoun workspace tests preserve v4.16.0 behaviour exactly (chain-difference cases are the 99 % of dialog); public API surface (`parse_input_with_priors` signature) identical. Pipeline: ~30-line comparator extension + 4 unit tests; no schema changes, no new artifacts, no new dependencies. Workspace tests **818 ‚Üí 822 passing** (+4 runtime priors tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ runtime layer opens.** Next: v4.22.5+ (live REPL transcript collection to verify chain-collision improvements show up in real dialog), v4.23.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.21.5 ‚ÄĒ pronoun paradigm extension (–Ī“Ī–Ľ / —Ā–ĺ–Ľ / –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ / —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ) + 4 new eval cases + —Ā–ĺ–Ľ lexicon entry.** Patch in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.21.0 shipped –ĺ–Ľ's 6 oblique cases as the architectural foundation; v4.21.5 extends the same mechanism to the rest of the demonstrative / personal closed class. **(1)** Paradigm table grew 6 ‚Üí 21 entries: –Ī“Ī–Ľ (6 oblique cases ‚ÄĒ same `–Ľ ‚Üí –Ĺ/“ď/–ī` lateralization), —Ā–ĺ–Ľ (6 cases ‚ÄĒ same pattern), –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ (only Dative –ľ–į“ď–į–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ others regular), —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ (only Dative —Ā–į“ď–į–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ same `—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ ‚Üí —Ā–į-` alternation). **(2)** `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json` += `pron_sol` ‚ÄĒ uncovered while running new —Ā–ĺ–Ľ eval cases: `analyse("—Ā–ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ")` previously returned only verb-root ¬ę—Ā–ĺ“ď–į¬Ľ (Reflexive paradigm) parses, no ¬ę—Ā–ĺ–Ľ + Dat¬Ľ, because –Īare —Ā–ĺ–Ľ wasn't in the lexicon at all (despite being a top-tier demonstrative pronoun). 1-line lexicon fix. **(3)** Eval test set extended +4 cases: bunda_anaphoric (–Ī“Ī–Ľ Loc), sogan_dative (—Ā–ĺ–Ľ Dat), magan_dative (–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ Dat), sagan_dative (—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ Dat). **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated ‚ÄĒ closed-class boost now applies to 6 of 10 entries (was 5 at v4.20.5; —Ā–ĺ–Ľ newly included). **Results (n=23):** baseline 78.3 %; chain-only strategies 91.3 % (improved from 89.5 % at v4.21.0 ‚ÄĒ chain priors handle most new cases without root help, because pronoun parses have higher chain prior scores than content-word alternatives); **chain_tiebreak_root 23/23 = 100.0 %**. All v4.21.0 –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į cases continue to resolve correctly + all 4 new v4.21.5 cases flip to their gold pronoun roots. Pipeline: paradigm table 6 ‚Üí 21 + 4 unit tests + segmentation_roots += pron_sol + eval JSON +4 cases + artifact regen + printout version. Workspace tests **814 ‚Üí 818 passing** (+4 pronoun_paradigm). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ measurement layer remains CLOSED at 100 % under extended test set.** Next: v4.22.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog ‚ÄĒ irregular noun stems, possessive-stem alternations, voicing edge cases).

**v4.21.0 ‚ÄĒ pronoun stem-alternation paradigm + 100 % accuracy on parse-disambiguation eval.** First minor in v4.21+ FST irregularity arc. v4.20.5's debug pass surfaced the actionable diagnosis: the FST returned no parse with root=`–ĺ–Ľ` for ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ because Kazakh's phonological alternation `–ĺ–Ľ ‚Üí –ĺ–Ĺ-` (lateralization `–Ľ ‚Üí –Ĺ` before consonant-initial dental suffixes) wasn't modelled. v4.21.0 ships the irregularity as a small hardcoded paradigm matcher and **closes the entire v4.19.0‚Äďv4.20.5 measurement arc with `chain_tiebreak_root` reaching 100 % accuracy on the parse-disambiguation eval**. **(1)** New module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/pronoun_paradigm.rs` ‚ÄĒ irregular-form table for Kazakh pronouns. v4.21.0 ships the `–ĺ–Ľ` paradigm (–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į / –ĺ–Ĺ—č / –ĺ–Ĺ—č“£ / –ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ / –ĺ–ī–į–Ĺ / –ĺ–Ĺ—č–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ 6 oblique cases). **(2)** `try_pronoun_paradigm(surface, lex)` consulted by `analyse()` after the regular noun/verb passes ‚ÄĒ strictly additive, no disturbance of existing candidates. The bare pronoun root is looked up via `lex.get(...)`; missing lexicon entry degrades silently. **Why hardcoded table not phonology rule:** general allomorph rules `–Ľ ‚Üí –Ĺ/“ď/–ī` would over-trigger on consonant-final nouns (–Ķ–Ľ ‚Üí *–Ķ–Ĺ-, –Ī–Ķ–Ľ ‚Üí *–Ī–Ķ–Ĺ-); linguistic reality is closed-class irregularity, exactly captured by listing the surface forms. **(3)** `pronoun_paradigm` exported from lib.rs for downstream extension. **(4)** Frozen priors artifact regenerated ‚ÄĒ –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į tokens now produce 2 distinct roots, correctly classified as ambiguous and skipped from root counting; closed-class boost (√ó10 from v4.20.5) keeps `P(–ĺ–Ľ)=-3.24 > P(–ĺ–Ĺ)=-5.06`. **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9 %; chain-only strategies 89.5 %; chain_plus_root 94.7 %; **chain_tiebreak_root 100.0 %** ‚ÄĒ both –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į cases (sentence-initial + mid-sentence) now correctly resolve to –ĺ–Ľ. **+21.1pp absolute lift over baseline.** This release closes a 6-release arc (v4.19.0 ‚Üí v4.21.0) that surfaced and resolved the chain-collision blind spot. The combined system: chain priors handle regular cases; root priors + closed-class boost provide the chain-collision tiebreaker; FST stem-alternation makes closed-class oblique forms available as candidates. Each layer has clear responsibility, clear-typed artifact, transparent eval reporting. Pipeline: 1 new module + 5 unit tests + analyse() augmented + lib.rs exports + artifact regen + eval JSON RESOLVED notes. Workspace tests **809‚Üí814 passing** (+5 pronoun_paradigm). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ measurement layer CLOSED at 100 %.** Next: v4.21.5 (extend paradigm with –Ī“Ī–Ľ / —Ā–ĺ–Ľ / –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ / —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ / –ľ—č–Ĺ–į—É / –į–Ĺ–į—É + new eval cases), v4.22.0+ (broader FST irregularity catalog).

**v4.20.5 ‚ÄĒ closed-class structural-pronoun boost + diagnostic discovery: –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į's gold parse isn't an FST candidate.** Patch in v4.20+ root-axis arc. Implements the closed-class boost planned by v4.20.0's writeup, then surfaces the **third (and most actionable) negative finding**: priors-side fixes were targeting the wrong layer the entire time. **(1) New** `data/lexicon/closed_class_root_boosts.json` ‚ÄĒ hand-curated multiplicative count boosts for structural pronouns (–ĺ–Ľ/–Ī“Ī–Ľ/—Ā–ĺ–Ľ/–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ/—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ/–ĺ–Ľ–į—Ä/–Ī—Ė–∑/—Ā—Ė–∑/–ĺ—Ā—č/–ľ—č–Ĺ–į—É/–į–Ĺ–į—É). Compensates for v4.20.0's pronoun under-counting. **(2)** Training binary updated ‚ÄĒ reads boost file (graceful fallback), applies multiplicative factor to `root_counts` AFTER unambiguous-only counting and BEFORE Laplace smoothing. **No schema bump** (still v4) ‚ÄĒ boost folds into existing `root_log_prob`. **(3)** Eval binary `ADAM_DEBUG_TIEBREAK=1` env-gated debug pass dumps per-parse chain key, chain score, root score, picked parse. **Boost validation:** `–ĺ–Ľ` flipped from -5.45 ‚Üí **-3.24** (now above `–ĺ–Ĺ` at -5.06); `–Ī“Ī–Ľ`: -5.09 ‚Üí -3.10; `—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ`: -6.96 ‚Üí -5.44. 5 of 10 boosted roots applied (other 5 never appeared unambiguously). Boost mechanism works as designed. **THE CRITICAL FINDING:** eval results unchanged ‚ÄĒ `chain_tiebreak_root` STILL picks `–ĺ–Ĺ` for both –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į cases. The debug logger reveals why: **the FST returns NO parse with `root=–ĺ–Ľ` for ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ**. Both candidates have `root=–ĺ–Ĺ`. The gold parse isn't even a candidate. Reason: ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ starts with ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ¬Ľ, not ¬ę–ĺ–Ľ¬Ľ. The FST's prefix-match on root surface forms never considers ¬ę–ĺ–Ľ¬Ľ (2 chars) for ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ (4 chars). Kazakh has phonological alternation `–ĺ–Ľ ‚Üí –ĺ–Ĺ-` before consonant-initial suffixes (locative `-–ī–į`, accusative `-–Ĺ—č`, dative `-“ď–į–Ĺ`) ‚ÄĒ regular lateralization. The lexicon has bare `–ĺ–Ľ` as a pronoun root, but the FST has no machinery to generate the `–ĺ–Ĺ-` allomorph during analysis. **Implication:** three releases of priors-side architecture (v4.19.0/v4.19.5/v4.20.0/v4.20.5) were looking in the wrong layer. The priors infrastructure stays in place for genuine chain-collision cases ‚ÄĒ but the –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į case can only be fixed at the FST/lexicon layer, not the scoring layer. This finding *unblocks* the project: eliminates an entire class of priors-tuning that would have continued to fail. Pipeline: 1 new data file + training binary boost-pass + eval debug logger + eval JSON notes updated. Workspace tests **809‚Üí809 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ root axis layer continues, but next step pivots OFF priors.** Next: v4.20.10 / v4.21.0 (FST stem-alternation for pronoun paradigm ‚ÄĒ add `–ĺ–Ĺ-`/`–ĺ“ď-`/`—Ā–ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ-`/`–ľ–į“ď–į–Ĺ-` allomorphs so –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į/–ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ/–ľ–į“ď–į–Ĺ/–Ī“Ī–Ĺ–ī–į surface the correct pronoun root as a candidate). Once the gold parse is *available*, v4.20.0's root prior + v4.20.5's closed-class boost will pick it under `chain_tiebreak_root` ‚ÄĒ at which point –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į finally flips.

**v4.20.0 ‚ÄĒ root-level priors + new prior axis (P(root) marginals via unambiguous-only attribution).** First minor in v4.20+ root-axis arc. v4.19.5 surfaced the structural finding that chain-level priors can't disambiguate root identity when both parses share a chain (–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į: `–ĺ–Ĺ+Loc` and `–ĺ–Ľ+Loc` collide). v4.20.0 builds the missing axis: a root-level marginal `P(root)` over the corpus, trained via **unambiguous-only attribution**, with two new evaluation strategies that combine it with the chain prior. **The empirical result is itself the second negative finding in a row** ‚ÄĒ but the architectural foundation is in place, the failure mode is precisely diagnosed, and the next steps are sharp. **(1) Schema bump v3 ‚Üí v4** ‚ÄĒ new `SuffixPriors::root_log_prob` field; `load()` rejects v3. **(2) New constructor `from_counts_with_bigrams_and_roots`** ‚ÄĒ third axis on top of v4.16/4.17 chain+bigram+POS. **(3) New method `score_root(root)`** ‚ÄĒ log P(root) with Laplace smoothing and floor. Empty-priors path returns 0.0 (additive identity). **(4) Training binary updated** ‚ÄĒ root counts via **unambiguous-only attribution**: token contributes to root only when `analyse()` returns parses with a single distinct root. Per v4.19.5 finding, uniform 1/N would dilute chain-collision pairs (–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į ‚Üí 0.5 –ĺ–Ĺ + 0.5 –ĺ–Ľ) ‚ÄĒ exactly where tiebreaker is needed. **(5) Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v4: 1112 chains, **9338 roots** from 3.3M unambiguous-token instances, 530K ambiguous skipped (~13.9% ambiguity rate). 1.5 MB JSON. **(6) Two new eval strategies:** `chain_plus_root` (additive log-prob), `chain_tiebreak_root` (strict tiebreaker). **Results (n=19):** baseline 78.9%; chain-only strategies 89.5%; **chain_plus_root REGRESSES to 84.2%** (high-frequency root ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ¬Ľ overrides correct chain pick); **chain_tiebreak_root holds at 89.5%** (no regression but no lift on –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į). **Why –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į still doesn't flip:** unambiguous-only attribution systematically under-counts pronouns. `–ĺ–Ľ` appears mostly in inherently-ambiguous forms (–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į, –ĺ–Ĺ—č, –ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ) which get filtered; digit `–ĺ–Ĺ` appears in many unambiguous numeric contexts (dates, ages). Result: corpus marginal `P(–ĺ–Ĺ) > P(–ĺ–Ľ)`, even though pronoun is far more common in real Kazakh. Fix paths: **closed-class boost** (v4.20.5 ‚ÄĒ hand-curate –ĺ–Ľ/–Ī“Ī–Ľ/—Ā–ĺ–Ľ/–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ/—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ/–ĺ–Ľ–į—Ä/–Ī—Ė–∑/—Ā—Ė–∑ with explicit prior boost), **lexical co-occurrence** `P(root | surrounding tokens)` (v4.21.0+), or **dialog-layer anaphor resolution** (bigger lift). Pipeline: schema v3‚Üív4 + 1 new field + 1 new constructor + 1 new method + 2 unit tests + training binary updated + frozen artifact regenerated + 2 new eval strategies. Workspace tests **807‚Üí809 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ root axis layer opens.** Next: v4.20.5 (closed-class structural-pronoun boost), v4.21.0+ (lexical co-occurrence if needed).

**v4.19.5 ‚ÄĒ sentence-context strategy + structural finding on root-vs-chain disambiguation.** Patch in v4.19+ measurement arc. v4.19.0 surfaced one residual failure (¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ gold = `–ĺ–Ľ + Loc` anaphoric, all isolated-token strategies pick `–ĺ–Ĺ + Loc` "in ten") and tagged it as needing "FST sentence-context plumbing." v4.19.5 builds that strategy and measures whether it actually helps. **It does not.** Publishable negative result ‚ÄĒ the structural reason gives a clearer architectural direction than blindly adding more context layers. **(1)** New `with_context` strategy as 6th tier in `eval_parse_disambiguation`: walks the full eval sentence left-to-right, greedily picking each token's parse under bigram-aware Jelinek-Mercer smoothed scoring (mirrors `parse_input_inner` in `adam-dialog`), tracks `prev_chain` across tokens, returns the root that won when target token reached. Pure inline impl in eval binary ‚ÄĒ no new public API, no production code change. **(2)** New eval case `onda_anaphoric_mid_sentence` ‚ÄĒ companion to `onda_must_not_be_ten_locative`. Same ambiguity, but –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į appears MID-SENTENCE (¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ī—č–ľ –Ī–į—Ä, –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į —Ā—É—Ä–Ķ—ā—ā–Ķ—Ä –ļ”©–Ņ.¬Ľ) ‚ÄĒ distinguishes "context unavailable" from "context available but unhelpful." **Results (n=19):** baseline 15/19 = 78.9%; all 5 prior strategies including with_context **17/19 = 89.5%**. `with_context` matches isolated-token strategies ‚ÄĒ **no additional lift**. Both –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į cases (sentence-initial AND mid-sentence) still pick –ĺ–Ĺ. **Why context plumbing doesn't help:** both `–ĺ–Ĺ + Locative` and `–ĺ–Ľ + Locative` produce the SAME suffix chain (`noun:None|Singular|None|Locative|None`). Chain-level priors ‚ÄĒ unigram, bigram, smoothed, POS-conditioned ‚ÄĒ score these two analyses **identically**. Stable lex order picks –ĺ–Ĺ. The runtime layer doing context-aware re-ranking can't fix this; the signal needs to come from a different axis ‚ÄĒ **root-level priors** `P(root | suffix_chain)`, lexical co-occurrence, or genuine anaphor resolution at the dialog layer. This reshapes v4.20+ direction: next compositional ML layer is about adding root-identity to the prior axis, not deeper context plumbing in the FST. Pipeline: 1 binary extension (~50 lines) + 1 new eval case + 1 updated note. No production code changes. Workspace tests **807‚Üí807 passing**. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ measurement layer continues.** Next: v4.20.0+ (root-level priors to break the chain-collision tie), v4.20.5+ (corpus expansion + retraining).

**v4.19.0 ‚ÄĒ empirical eval of v4.15+ priors.** First minor in the v4.19+ measurement arc, long-deferred from v4.17.5. v4.15.0 ‚Üí v4.17.0 shipped four prior strategies (unigram ‚Üí bigram ‚Üí smoothed ‚Üí POS-conditioned) with anecdotal REPL evidence but no measured accuracy. v4.19.0 closes that loop. **Architectural addition:** `data/eval/parse_disambiguation_eval.json` ‚ÄĒ 20 hand-labeled cases of ambiguous Kazakh surface forms drawn from past live-REPL bugs (v3.9.5 –Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ĺ ‚Üí –Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ, v4.3.5 –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į ‚Üí –ĺ–Ĺ, v4.4.10 “õ—č—Ā“õ–į—Ā—č / –Ķ—ą—ā–Ķ“£–Ķ) plus cross-domain ambiguous content nouns (—ā—Ė–Ľ, –ļ”©–∑, —ą–į–Ļ, –ļ“Į–Ļ, —ā–į—Ā, –Ī–į—Ä, –ļ–Ķ–Ľ, —ā–į—É, —ą”©–Ľ, –Ķ–Ľ, –ļ“Į–Ĺ, –ļ”©–Ņ, ”©–∑, “õ–į–∑–į, –į–Ľ–ľ–į, –∂–ĺ“õ). Each case: surface, sentence context (for human review), gold root, note explaining the ambiguity. **New binary** `eval_parse_disambiguation` in `adam-corpus`: loads eval set + Lexicon + trained `SuffixPriors`, runs `analyse()` per token, applies five scoring strategies (baseline lexicographic / unigram v4.15.5 / bigram v4.16.0 / smoothed v4.16.5 őĪ=0.3 / POS-conditioned v4.17.0), reports per-strategy accuracy + per-case detail (`=` / `‚ö†` markers). **Results (n=18 with non-empty FST parses):** baseline **15/18 = 83.3%**; all four prior strategies **17/18 = 94.4%** ‚ÄĒ **+11.1 pp lift from priors over the lexicographic baseline**. The four prior strategies collapse to identical scores on isolated tokens (no preceding chain ‚Üí bigram/smoothed/POS-conditioned all fall back to unigram) ‚ÄĒ sanity check that higher-order tiers don't *regress* on no-context queries. Two cases where priors flip the wrong baseline pick: ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ĺ¬Ľ (baseline picks `–Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ + Abl`, priors pick bare `–Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ĺ`) and ¬ę–į–Ľ–ľ–į¬Ľ (baseline picks verb `–į–Ľ`, priors pick noun `–į–Ľ–ľ–į` = apple). One residual failure (all strategies): ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ gold = `–ĺ–Ľ + Loc` (anaphoric "there"), priors pick `–ĺ–Ĺ + Loc` ("in ten") ‚ÄĒ needs sentence context, beyond isolated-token scope. Two cases skipped (`“õ–į–∑–į`, `”©–∑`) ‚ÄĒ `analyse()` returns no parses; logged to stderr, removed from accuracy denominator. Pipeline: 1 new eval data file + 1 new binary + 1 `[[bin]]` registration. **No runtime code changes** ‚ÄĒ pure infrastructure / measurement. Workspace tests **806‚Üí807 passing**. Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ measurement layer.** Next: v4.19.5+ (FST sentence-context plumbing for `–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į`-class disambiguation), v4.20.0+ (corpus expansion + retraining priors over larger token base).

New template family `ask_about_system.intro_and_capabilities` surfaces both `system_kind` AND `system_capabilities` in sequence. Closes 2026-05-01 transcript turn 4 ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č, –ļ—Ė–ľ –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£—Ė–∑ –∂”ô–Ĺ–Ķ –Ĺ–Ķ —Ė—Ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—ā—č–Ĺ—č“£—č–∑ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –į–Ļ—ā—č“£—č–∑¬Ľ where adam previously answered only the first half. **(2)** New `name_respect_distinct` slot ‚ÄĒ set ONLY when respect form differs from literal name (consonant-initial only). Gated on `{name_respect_distinct}` so it auto-filters for vowel-initial names (–ź–Ī–į–Ļ ‚Üí name_respect = literal ‚Üí no distinct form, no awkward ¬ę–°—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –ź–Ī–į–Ļ –ī–Ķ–Ņ –į—ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ). For consonant-initial names (–Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā/–ú–į—Ä–į—ā/–°–Ķ—Ä—Ė–ļ) the user sees they were heard verbatim AND learns adam's address style with explicit cultural note. **v4.18.0 ‚ÄĒ respectful Kazakh address (–Ē”ô–ļ–Ķ/–ú”ô–ļ–Ķ/–°”ô–ļ–Ķ) + list-class DialogContext tracking.** First minor in v4.18+. Two architectural additions explicitly directed by the user during v4.17.5 review. **(1) Respectful Kazakh address** ‚ÄĒ per Kazakh tradition a junior speaker addresses an older / honored person by ¬ę<first-consonant>”ô–ļ–Ķ¬Ľ (–Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā ‚Üí –Ē”ô–ļ–Ķ, –ú–į—Ä–į—ā ‚Üí –ú”ô–ļ–Ķ, –°–Ķ—Ä—Ė–ļ ‚Üí –°”ô–ļ–Ķ). Adam is a young system addressing the human user ‚ÄĒ every post-introduction turn now uses the diminutive form. New `kazakh_respectful_address(name) -> Option<String>` helper in language_core (vowel-initial names like –ź–Ī–į–Ļ return None, fall back to literal). New `is_kazakh_vowel(c)` covers all native Kazakh vowels. After `StatementOfName`, session stores BOTH `name` (literal) AND `name_respect` (diminutive). New `ensure_name_respect_slot` planner helper auto-derives respect form from name for direct-session-insert callers (tests/replay). 28 templates migrated to `{name_respect}`; 5 literal-name templates kept (first-ack warmth + `ask_name.with_known_user` recall). The split: first turn uses literal so user sees they were heard verbatim, subsequent turns use respect for warmth. **(2) List-class DialogContext tracking** ‚ÄĒ closes v4.17.5 known limitation. After each turn renders, `Conversation::turn_with_trace` stashes the rendered grounded_fact in session (cleared on no-grounded turns). `ToolContext` gains `previous_grounded_fact: Option<&'a str>`. `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` `list_intent_rank` extends with 4-tier fallback ladder: synonym query‚Üíobject ‚Üí synonym prev-fact‚Üíobject ‚Üí direct prev-fact-class‚Üíobject ‚Üí unmatched. Closes the ¬ę–ě–Ľ–į—Ä–ī—č —ā—Ė–∑—Ė–ľ–ī–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ case where adam previously surfaced rivers; now correctly surfaces the regions list because previous turn mentioned ¬ę–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā¬Ľ. 4 unit tests + 2 REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 1 new pub function + 2 new helpers (`is_kazakh_vowel`, `ensure_name_respect_slot`) + ToolContext +1 field + 28 template migrations + 5 end_to_end tests broadened to accept either form. Workspace tests **802‚Üí806 passing**. **Stripe (5) ‚ÄĒ humanness through cultural fit ‚ÄĒ opens.** Next: v4.18.5 (composite-question handler ¬ęX –∂”ô–Ĺe Y¬Ľ two-aspect splitter + intro warmth combining literal + respect: ¬ę–Ę–į–Ĺ—č—Ā“õ–į–Ĺ—č–ľ–į “õ—É–į–Ĺ—č—ą—ā—č–ľ—č–Ĺ, {name}! –°—Ė–∑–ī—Ė {name_respect} –ī–Ķ–Ņ –į—ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ “õ–į–∑–į“õ –ī”ô—Ā—ā“Į—Ä—Ė –Ī–ĺ–Ļ—č–Ĺ—ą–į.¬Ľ), v4.19.0+ (empirical eval of v4.15+ priors).

**v4.17.5 ‚ÄĒ transcript-driven patch bundle (11 fixes from live REPL session).** Patch in the v4.x humanness arc.
