**v4.17.0 ‚ÄĒ POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain) + 4-tier fallback ladder.** Third minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 added bigrams, v4.16.5 added Jelinek-Mercer smoothing. v4.17.0 adds the **POS-aggregated fallback tier** ‚ÄĒ when a full bigram row is sparse but the previous token's POS is known, fall back to the POS-conditioned distribution before dropping to the unigram. Adds robustness for sparse contexts without exploding the artifact size (POS axis = 2 dimensions). **Architectural addition:** new field `SuffixPriors::pos_transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` keyed by POS string (`"noun"` / `"verb"`) ‚Üí curr_chain ‚Üí log_prob. Schema bumped 2‚Üí3. **(1)** `from_counts_with_bigrams` extended to compute POS-aggregated rows in parallel with full bigrams (zero extra training cost ‚ÄĒ same pass). **(2)** New helpers: `pos_from_chain_key(chain)` extracts POS prefix; `smooth_row(row)` extracted for code reuse. **(3)** Extended `score_chain_given_prev` 4-tier fallback ladder: **full bigram ‚Üí POS-bigram ‚Üí unigram ‚Üí floor**. POS-bigram tier inserted when full-bigram row is empty OR sparse (curr unseen). Strictly additive: rich-context behaviour identical to v4.16.5. **(4)** SCHEMA_VERSION 2‚Üí3. **(5)** Training binary write_priors extracts `serialize_nested_map` helper used for both transition and POS-transition serialisation. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog. **Frozen artifact regenerated** at schema v3: 1112 chains, 21270 full bigrams across 711 prev rows, **846 POS-bigrams across 2 dense rows** (noun: 423 successors, verb: 423 successors). 1.4 MB JSON (POS adds ~16 KB ‚ÄĒ total artifact size effectively unchanged). Anti-regression 11/11 ‚ÄĒ POS-bigrams only fire on sparse-bigram-row paths, which canonical queries don't walk. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field, score_chain_given_prev +1 fallback tier, training binary refactored. Workspace tests **799‚Üí802 passing** (+3 unit tests). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ fallback ladder layer.** Next: v4.17.5 (empirical eval ‚ÄĒ tiny held-out test set of FST-ambiguous tokens with hand-labelled correct readings, measure how often v4.16.0/v4.16.5/v4.17.0 each pick the labelled parse vs raw v3.2.0 lexicographic).

**v4.16.5 ‚ÄĒ Jelinek-Mercer interpolation knob őĪ¬∑log_p_unigram + (1-őĪ)¬∑log_p_bigram.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.16.0 shipped pure bigram scoring with three-tier fallback. v4.16.5 adds the **smoothing dial**: a tunable interpolation weight between unigram and bigram log-probabilities. Lets the runtime balance the bigram's specificity (good when context is rich) against the unigram's robustness (good when bigram rows are sparse). **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::score_chain_smoothed(curr, prev, alpha)` + `score_noun_smoothed` + `score_verb_smoothed` ‚ÄĒ Jelinek-Mercer interpolation `őĪ¬∑log P(curr) + (1-őĪ)¬∑log P(curr|prev)`. `őĪ` clamped to [0,1]. Symmetric early-outs for `őĪ‚Čą0` and `őĪ‚Čą1` keep the hot path fast. **(2)** New `Conversation::with_priors_alpha(őĪ)` builder + `priors_alpha: Option<f32>` field. `None` preserves v4.16.0 pure-bigram-with-fallback path; `Some(őĪ)` switches re-ranker to interpolation mode. **(3)** `parse_input_with_priors` signature extended with `alpha: Option<f32>`; all 4 call sites updated. Older callers passing only `priors` get bit-identical behaviour. **(4)** `adam_chat` defaults to `őĪ = 0.3` (bigram-dominant with unigram smoothing). **Tunable via `ADAM_PRIORS_ALPHA` env var** for experimentation without recompilation. Startup line announces the chosen alpha. **(5)** 3 new unit tests (őĪ=0 = pure bigram, őĪ=1 = pure unigram, out-of-range clamps). **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers single-noun (minimal bigram) + multi-token (rich bigram) queries ‚ÄĒ both must answer correctly under smoothing. **Why őĪ=0.3:** textbook Jelinek-Mercer for bigrams under Laplace-smoothed counts; bigram dominates (70%), unigram smooths sparse rows (30%). Empirically verified on 11-question anti-regression battery ‚ÄĒ v4.16.0 behaviour preserved on every canonical query while making prior more robust to unseen contexts. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +3 methods, Conversation +1 field +1 builder, parse_input chain extended with alpha, adam_chat startup attaches őĪ=0.3 with env override. Workspace tests **796‚Üí799 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 REPL replay). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ smoothing patch.** Next: v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors `P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)` for sparse-mitigation).

**v4.16.0 ‚ÄĒ context-aware priors P(chain | preceding_chain) + greedy bigram-aware FST parse selection.** Second minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped unigram priors `P(chain)`, v4.15.5 wired them into runtime parse selection. v4.16.0 extends to **context-aware bigrams** `P(chain | preceding_chain)` ‚ÄĒ captures local morphological agreement (e.g. Genitive followed by 3sg-Possessive ‚ÄĒ ¬ę–∂–į—Ā—É—ą–į–Ĺ—č“£ —Ź–ī—Ä–ĺ—Ā—č¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ is much more probable than Genitive followed by Imperative). Same `–ļ–ĺ—Ä–Ķ–Ĺ—Ć + —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź^n` compositional view, one Markov step deeper. **(1)** New `SuffixPriors::transition_log_prob: HashMap<String, HashMap<String, f32>>` field keyed by `(prev_chain, curr_chain)`. SCHEMA_VERSION bumped 1 ‚Üí 2; v1 artifacts rejected by `load()`. **(2)** New `from_counts_with_bigrams` constructor with row-local add-one smoothing. **(3)** New `score_chain_given_prev` / `score_noun_given_prev` / `score_verb_given_prev` API with three-tier fallback ladder (no prev ‚Üí unigram, unseen prev ‚Üí unigram, unseen pair in known prev row ‚Üí row floor). **(4)** Training binary updated with two-pass algorithm: first pass builds unique-token ‚Üí chain-keys cache, second pass walks samples in order and tallies bigrams using the cache. Bigram pruning (count < 2.0) drops single-occurrence noise ‚ÄĒ 305K observed pairs ‚Üí 21K retained, ~6√ó artifact size reduction. **(5)** Greedy bigram-aware parse selection in `parse_input_inner` ‚ÄĒ tracks the previous token's selected chain key, passes it into `score_chain_given_prev` when re-ranking candidates. Sentence starts / FST-empty tokens reset context. Stable sort preserves v3.2.0 lexicographic order on equal-prior parses. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog covers multi-token queries where bigram context matters. **Frozen artifact regenerated** as schema v2: 5,765,342 tokens, 1,112 chains, 305,856 bigrams observed ‚Üí 21,270 retained, 711 transition rows; 1.4 MB JSON (was 70 KB unigram-only, well under 50 MB gitignore policy). 11-question anti-regression battery passes ‚ÄĒ bigram-aware re-rank doesn't disturb any v4.x behaviour. Pipeline: SuffixPriors +1 field + 1 constructor + 3 API methods, SCHEMA_VERSION bump, training-binary upgrade, runtime integration. Workspace tests **793‚Üí796 passing** (+3 unit tests + 1 schema-version assertion bumped). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ context-aware step.** Next: v4.16.5 (smoothing/interpolation knob őĪ¬∑log_p_unigram + (1-őĪ)¬∑log_p_bigram), v4.17.0 (POS-conditioned priors P(chain | prev_pos, prev_chain)).

**v4.15.5 ‚ÄĒ SuffixPriors runtime integration: priors-aware FST parse selection.** Patch in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. v4.15.0 shipped the trained `SuffixPriors` artifact + `load`/`score` API but explicitly deferred runtime integration to keep the architectural addition reversible. v4.15.5 wires the prior into the parse pipeline as a re-ranking signal: each turn's FST candidate analyses are now sorted by `P(chain)` DESC before downstream consumers see them. **Strictly additive** ‚ÄĒ when no priors are attached, the v3.2.0 deterministic lexicographic order is preserved bit-for-bit. **(1)** New `parse_input_with_priors` in lib.rs uses a stable comparator: parses scored higher by `P(chain)` move forward, ties retain the v3.2.0 lexicographic order. **(2)** `Conversation.suffix_priors: Option<SuffixPriors>` field + `with_suffix_priors(priors)` builder. **(3)** `Conversation::turn_with_trace` calls `parse_input_with_priors` with `self.suffix_priors.as_ref()`, threading the optional prior through the existing parse path. **(4)** `adam_chat` startup loads priors from `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` (the v4.15.0 artifact), validates schema version, attaches via builder. Production startup now logs all four context layers: morpheme index, reasoning facts, domain index, **suffix priors (1112 chains over 5.77M training tokens)**. **(5)** Public exports tightened in adam-kernel-fst::lib. **(6)** 1 new REPL replay regression dialog locks v4.x baseline behaviour through the priors pipeline. Pipeline: 1 new lib function + new Conversation field + new builder + adam_chat startup integration. Cadence: patch. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ first runtime patch.** Next: v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)` capturing local morphological agreement ‚ÄĒ one Markov step deeper, same compositional view).

**v4.15.0 ‚ÄĒ first compositional ML layer: P(suffix_chain) priors + offline training pass.** First minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. The Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix_1 + suffix_2 + ... + suffix_n`). Pre-v4.15.0 the FST analyser returned candidate parses in deterministic lexicographic order (v3.2.0 contract), but had no notion of which suffix-chains are actually *common* in Kazakh usage. v4.15.0 adds the missing distributional signal as a frozen, trained-offline prior over chain signatures, ready to inform downstream tie-breaking from v4.15.5 onward. Infrastructure-only release: the prior is loaded but not yet integrated into runtime decision-making ‚ÄĒ splitting the architectural addition from the behaviour change keeps both reversible. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/suffix_priors.rs` (~280 lines + 8 tests). `struct SuffixPriors { version, trained_on_tokens, chain_log_prob }` ‚ÄĒ frozen lookup table from chain signature (e.g. `noun:None|Singular|None|Locative|None`) to natural-log probability. `SuffixPriors::load(path)` validates schema version (1 at v4.15.0). `SuffixPriors::from_counts` builds the prior with add-one (Laplace) smoothing. `score_noun` / `score_verb` are single hashmap probes. Unseen chains return `min_observed - ln(2)` so they rank strictly below the rarest observed chain. **Training pass:** new binary `crates/adam-corpus/src/bin/train_suffix_priors.rs`. Walks every `data/curated/*.json` pack, runs FST analyse on each token, attributes uniform `1/N` weight to each candidate parse (uniform attribution ‚ÄĒ unbiased given no labels), tallies counts, hands them to `SuffixPriors::from_counts`, writes `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` as deterministic pretty-printed JSON (sorted keys for byte-stable output). **Why uniform attribution:** picking only the first parse would make the prior a circular reflection of the existing tie-breaker; uniform attribution captures which suffix chains *appear at all* in real Kazakh text. **Per the user's directive (`project_v4_direction`):** Predictable (pure frequency count, no embeddings/SGD), Cheap (5-min one-off training, single hashmap probe at runtime), Safe (only ranks pre-existing FST parses, never invents new ones), Foundation (preserves the `–ļ–ĺ—Ä–Ķ–Ĺ—Ć + —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź^n` view, version-bump path is built in). Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 frozen artifact + new dep edge `adam-corpus ‚Üí adam-kernel-fst`. Workspace tests **785‚Üí793 passing** (+8). Cadence: minor. **Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ opens.** Next: v4.15.5 (runtime integration in `best_noun_hint` as tiebreaker), v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)`).

**v4.14.5 ‚ÄĒ predicate decomposition wiring + domain-aware retrieval reranker.** Patch in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 introduced `sentence_decomp` (case-role decomposition) and v4.14.0 introduced `DomainIndex` + `DialogContext.current_domain`. v4.14.5 wires both into the runtime path so they actually influence behavior ‚ÄĒ strictly additive, no regression risk. **(1)** Domain-aware retrieval tiebreaker ‚ÄĒ `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` sort cascade gains a new tier between `user_facing_fact_priority` and `raw_text length`: when both `current_domain` AND `domain_index` are attached, candidates whose subject's primary domain matches the currently-discussed domain win over equal-priority candidates from other domains. Useful for cross-domain ambiguous topics (`—ā—Ė–Ľ` linguistics OR biology body part, `–ļ”©–∑` biology OR geography spring, `—Ā–į–Ļ` botany OR geography). Strictly additive ‚ÄĒ only fires on ties. **(2)** `ToolContext` extended with `current_domain: Option<&'a str>` + `domain_index: Option<&'a DomainIndex>`. Both `Some` only when v4.14.0+ wiring is attached; older callers pass `None`/empty index, preserving pre-v4.14.5 behaviour bit-for-bit. **(3)** `Conversation::turn_with_trace` wires new fields. Empty-index short-circuit means tiebreaker doesn't even run when index has nothing to say. **(4)** `sentence_decomp` focus fallback in `interpret_text_with_lexicon` ‚ÄĒ when greedy `best_noun_hint` returns None, `sentence_decomp::decompose` runs; if its `focus` is set AND `focus_role ‚ąą {Subject, Object, Source, Locus}`, it becomes the noun_hint. Strictly additive. Predicate-role focus excluded so a bare verb root is never promoted as topic. **(5)** NOT_A_TOPIC re-check on the fallback path ‚ÄĒ fixed an early v4.14.5 regression where sentence_decomp fallback bypassed v4.4.10 closed-class additions (`“õ—č—Ā“õ–į`, `–Ķ—ą—ā–Ķ“£–Ķ`, etc) because sentence_decomp keeps its own smaller list. The re-check applies the full `NOT_A_TOPIC` filter, restoring `qysqasy_does_not_get_extracted_as_topic`. **(6)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: ToolContext +2 fields + new domain-match tiebreaker tier + new fallback path; workspace tests **785‚Üí785 passing** (+2 REPL replay dialogs). Cadence: patch. **Stripe (3) ‚ÄĒ domain awareness ‚ÄĒ final patch closes the architectural-wiring gap.** Next: v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.14.0 ‚ÄĒ DomainIndex foundation + DialogContext.current_domain wiring + curriculum-content honest fallback.** Third minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 introduced `DialogContext` with `current_domain` slot but left it always `None` (no topic‚Üídomain mapping). v4.14.0 builds the missing index, wires it through `Conversation`, and adds the third 2026-05-01 transcript failure handler. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/domain_index.rs` (~150 lines): `DomainIndex { by_topic: HashMap<String, String> }` ‚ÄĒ topic root ‚Üí primary World-Core domain. `DomainIndex::build(entries)` walks every fact, tallies (root, domain) counts; primary = majority winner with alphabetical tie-break for full determinism. `DomainIndex::lookup_domain(topic)` is case-insensitive O(1). Built once at `adam_chat` startup from `data/world_core/*.jsonl` ‚ÄĒ **1 644 topics indexed across 38 domains**. **(1)** New `Conversation::with_domain_index(idx)` builder + per-turn `DialogContext.current_domain` population via `domain_index.lookup_domain(noun_hint)`. The existing v4.13.0 majority-vote logic (`recompute_domain` over the last DOMAIN_WINDOW=4 turns) settles `current_domain` on the currently-discussed subject area. **(2)** `adam_chat` startup integration ‚ÄĒ loads world_core via `adam_reasoning::world_core::load_world_core_dir`, builds index, attaches via builder. Failure to load is non-fatal (empty index, no-ops cleanly). **(3)** New `Intent::AskCurriculumContent` variant + detector + template family `ask_curriculum_content`. Pattern: subject (student-class: `–ĺ“õ—É—ą—č / —Ā—ā—É–ī–Ķ–Ĺ—ā / —ą”ô–ļ—Ė—Ä—ā`) + education locus (`–ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ / —Ā–į–Ī–į“õ / —Ā—č–Ĺ—č–Ņ—ā–į / —É–Ĺ–ł–≤–Ķ—Ä—Ā–ł—ā–Ķ—ā / –ļ–ĺ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ī–∂`) + question word `–Ĺ–Ķ` + learning verb (`–ĺ“õ–ł–ī—č / “Į–Ļ—Ä–Ķ–Ĺ–Ķ–ī—Ė / –ĺ“õ–ł—Ā—č“£ / –ĺ“õ–ł—Ā—č–∑ / ...`). Conservative ‚ÄĒ requires ALL four signals so generic ¬ę–ĺ“õ—É—ą—č —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ doesn't accidentally route here. Catches ¬ę–ě“õ—É—ą—č–Ľ–į—Ä –ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ—ā–Ķ —Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į –Ņ”ô–Ĺ—Ė–Ĺ–Ķ–Ĺ –Ĺ–Ķ –ĺ“õ–ł–ī—č?¬Ľ and ¬ę–°—ā—É–ī–Ķ–Ĺ—ā—ā–Ķ—Ä —É–Ĺ–ł–≤–Ķ—Ä—Ā–ł—ā–Ķ—ā—ā–Ķ –Ĺ–Ķ –ĺ“õ–ł–ī—č?¬Ľ. Pre-v4.14.0 surfaced greedy IsA fact about `–ĺ“õ—É—ą—č`. Honest fallback: ¬ę–Ď“Ī–Ľ —Ā“Ī—Ä–į“ď—č“£—č–∑ –ĺ“õ—É –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č–Ĺ—č“£ –ľ–į–∑–ľ“Ī–Ĺ—č–Ĺ–į “õ–į—ā—č—Ā—ā—č ‚ÄĒ –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ–ī–Ķ –Ĺ–į“õ—ā—č –Ņ”ô–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ļ –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ –∂–ĺ“õ. –ú–Ķ–Ĺ ”ô—Ä –Ņ”ô–Ĺ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –Ĺ–Ķ –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė–Ĺ, –Ĺ–Ķ–≥—Ė–∑–≥—Ė “Ī“ď—č–ľ–ī–į—Ä—č –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –ľ–į“£—č–∑–ī—č –į—ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä—č–Ĺ –į–Ļ—ā—č–Ņ –Ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ –į–Ľ–į–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ. **(4)** New `IntentKind::AskCurriculumContent` companion variant. **(5)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 1 new module + new Conversation field + new Intent variant + new template family + DomainIndex now actually populated (was always None pre-v4.14.0); workspace tests **777‚Üí785 passing** (+8 domain_index unit tests). **All three 2026-05-01 transcript failures now closed across v4.13.0/v4.13.5/v4.14.0.** Stripe (3) ‚ÄĒ domain awareness ‚ÄĒ opens. Next: v4.14.5 (predicate decomposition wiring + domain-aware retrieval reranker), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.13.5 ‚ÄĒ capability honest fallbacks: generic verb-capability + multi-topic capability detection.** Patch in the v4.12+ humanness arc. v4.13.0 laid the foundation (sentence_decomp + DialogContext + closed-class hygiene) and intentionally deferred the answer-side work; v4.13.5 closes the two known gaps explicitly listed in the v4.13.0 release notes by adding two new `SystemAspect` variants. **(1)** `SystemAspect::GenericCapability` + detector for `<verb-converb> –į–Ľ–į<person> <–ľ–į/–Ī–į/–Ņ–į>?` pattern ‚ÄĒ surface forms `–į–Ľ–į—Ā—č“£/–į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į/–ľ–į`, `–į–Ľ–į –ľ–į?`, `–į–Ľ–į–ī—č –ľ–į`. Distinct from `Capabilities` (v4.6.0 ‚ÄĒ language-only with closed adverb prefix) and `Limitations` (v4.6.0 ‚ÄĒ `–į–Ľ–ľ–į–Ļ—Ā—č“£/–į–Ľ–ľ–į–Ļ—Ā—č–∑`). Catches ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į –∂–į–∑–į –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ, ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –Ķ—Ā–Ķ–Ņ—ā–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ, ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –ĺ–Ĺ—č –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ (now resolves `–ĺ–Ĺ—č ‚Üí Rust` via v4.13.0 DialogContext, then routes to GenericCapability). **(2)** `SystemAspect::MultiTopicCapability` + detector for 2+ commas (counted on raw input ‚ÄĒ `joined` strips punctuation) + `–∂”ô–Ĺ–Ķ` + `–Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė“£/–Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑`. Catches ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –ľ–į—ā–Ķ–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–į, —Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į, —Ö–ł–ľ–ł—Ź... –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑ –Ī–Ķ?¬Ľ. Pre-v4.13.5 surfaced `–ú–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ ‚ÄĒ –Ī—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ –Ī–Ķ—Ä—É –ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė`. **(3)** `detect_ask_about_system` signature extended with `raw_input: &str` so punctuation-sensitive detectors (comma-count) can run. **(4)** Two new fields on `SystemIdentity` (`generic_capability_summary` ~80 words + `multi_topic_capability_summary` ~50 words) + 2 new template families. **All three 2026-05-01 transcript failures now closed.** Pipeline: 2 new SystemAspect variants + 2 new SystemIdentity fields + 2 new template families + 11 new surface-form patterns. Workspace tests: 777 ‚Üí **777 passing** (+2 REPL replay dialogs). Cadence: patch (v4.13.5). **Stripe (2) ‚ÄĒ humanness ‚ÄĒ final patch.** Next: v4.14.0 (predicate decomposition + domain-TF-IDF + semantic-cohesion graph traversal), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer: `P(suffix_chain)` priors).

**v4.13.0 ‚ÄĒ sentence-decomposition foundation + DialogContext multi-turn topic memory + closed-class hygiene.** Second minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. The 2026-05-01 live-REPL transcript surfaced two systemic gaps: (a) **greedy first-noun-match** ‚ÄĒ modal particles / negators (`”ô–Ľ—Ė / ”ô–Ľ–ī–Ķ / –ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ / —ā–į“ď—č / –∂–ĺ“õ / –ł”ô / –Ņ–į / –Ņ–Ķ`) leaked into noun_hint as if they were content nouns, surfacing poetry; (b) **goldfish memory** ‚ÄĒ only one back-reference (`session["last_query_topic"]`) was tracked, so a turn referring to a topic from 3-4 turns earlier could not be resolved. v4.13.0 lays foundation for both. **Architectural addition #1** ‚ÄĒ new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/sentence_decomp.rs` (~470 lines): the Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix-chain` where each case suffix is `Noun ‚Üí CaseMarkedNoun[Role]`); FST already decomposes this, downstream code finally USES it. `enum SentenceType { Question, Statement, Imperative, Exclamation }` + `enum Role` (11 variants: Subject/Object/Locus/Source/Recipient/Possessor/Instrument/Predicate/QuestionWord/Closed/Coord) + `struct SentenceDecomposition { sentence_type, tokens, question_word, focus, focus_role, predicate, topic_list, cohesion }` + `fn decompose(input, parses, last_topic)` ‚ÄĒ pure function, O(n) over tokens, hardmap lookups only, microseconds per query. Question-word focus override: `–Ĺ–Ķ` asks for OBJECT, `“õ–į–Ļ–ī–į` LOCUS, `“õ–į—ą–į–Ĺ/“õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ/–Ĺ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ĺ` PREDICATE, `–ļ—Ė–ľ/“õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ` SUBJECT. **Architectural addition #2** ‚ÄĒ new module `crates/adam-dialog/src/dialog_context.rs` (~250 lines): `DialogContext { topic_history: Vec<TopicMention>, last_topic, subject_under_discussion, current_domain }` with capped FIFO history (MAX_HISTORY=64), majority-vote subject inference over STICKY_WINDOW=6 turns (one-off mentions don't displace), majority-vote domain over DOMAIN_WINDOW=4 turns. `resolve_anaphor()` consults `subject_under_discussion` first, falls back to `last_topic`. New `Conversation.dialog_context` field, updated each turn after Intent::Unknown.noun_hint resolves. **(1)** Closed-class additions to `NOT_A_TOPIC`: 8 entries (`”ô–Ľ—Ė / ”ô–Ľ–ī–Ķ / –ľ“Į–ľ–ļ—Ė–Ĺ / —ā–į“ď—č / –∂–ĺ“õ / –ł”ô / –Ņ–į / –Ņ–Ķ` ‚ÄĒ modal/discourse particles + existential negator + post-voiceless allomorphs of question particle, completing the `–ľ–į/–ľ–Ķ/–Ī–į/–Ī–Ķ/–Ņ–į/–Ņ–Ķ` paradigm). **(2)** Acc/Dat/Gen anaphor extension to `DISCOURSE_ANAPHORS`: 12 forms (`–ĺ–Ĺ—č/—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ—č/–ľ“Ī–Ĺ—č/–Ī“Ī–Ĺ—č/–ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ/—Ā–ĺ“ď–į–Ĺ/–ľ“Ī“ď–į–Ĺ/–Ī“Ī“ď–į–Ĺ/–ĺ–Ĺ—č“£/—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ—č“£/–ľ“Ī–Ĺ—č“£/–Ī“Ī–Ĺ—č“£`) ‚ÄĒ pre-v4.13.0 only Loc + Abl cases were registered, so ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –ĺ–Ĺ—č –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į?¬Ľ (¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ—č¬Ľ = "it" Acc) was ignored. **(3)** Multi-turn anaphora live-test: turn 1 ¬ęRust —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑ –Ī–Ķ?¬Ľ establishes Rust as topic; turn 2 ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ –ĺ–Ĺ—č...¬Ľ now resolves ¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ—č ‚Üí Rust¬Ľ via DialogContext. **(4)** 2 new REPL replay regression dialogs. Pipeline: 2 new modules + new `Conversation` field + 12 closed-class entries + 12 anaphor forms; workspace tests **758‚Üí777 passing** (+19: 11 sentence_decomp unit tests + 8 dialog_context unit tests). **Zero ML.** Probabilistic suffix-chain prior (`P(suffix_chain)` ‚ÄĒ natural `root + function^n` learning) reserved for v4.15+. Next: v4.13.5 (generic capability detector + honest fallback templates), v4.14.0 (predicate decomposition + domain-TF-IDF), v4.15.0 (first compositional ML layer).

**v4.12.0 ‚ÄĒ humanness milestone: question-shape classifier + Implementation aspect + causal-reasoning routing + backtick carve-out for user output.** First minor in the v4.12+ humanness research arc. Stripe (1) ‚ÄĒ "answer-by-the-point" ‚ÄĒ closed across all 38 world_core domains in v4.11.5/.6/.7; v4.12.0 opens stripe (2) ‚ÄĒ "human-like reasoning" ‚ÄĒ by giving the planner an analytical signal it never had: the **form** of the user's question (definition vs causal vs listing vs comparison vs yes/no), independent of topic. **Architectural addition:** new `crates/adam-dialog/src/question_shape.rs` module with `QuestionShape` enum (5 variants: Definition, Causal, YesNoCheck, Listing, Comparison) + pure surface-level `detect(input) -> Option<QuestionShape>`; new `Intent::Unknown.question_shape: Option<QuestionShape>` field populated at the top of `interpret_text_with_lexicon`; preserved across `verifier::strip_evidence`. **(1)** New `SystemAspect::Implementation` variant + detector for ¬ę–°—Ė–∑ “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī–Ķ –∂–į–∑—č–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ě–Ķ —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė–Ĺ–ī–Ķ –∂–į—Ā–į–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ—Ā—č“£?¬Ľ / ¬ę“ö–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė–Ĺ–ī–Ķ –∂–į–∑—č–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ?¬Ľ + template family `ask_about_system.implementation` rendering new `SystemIdentity::implementation_summary` (mentions `Rust`, the crate stack `adam-kernel/tokenizer/dialog/reasoning/retrieval/corpus`, FST + rule-based architecture, `macOS`/`Linux` platform support). Closes the v4.11.7 known gap. **(2)** Causal-reasoning routing ‚ÄĒ when `Intent::Unknown` carries `QuestionShape::Causal`, the planner short-circuits to `unknown.causal.with_fact` (grounded_fact present) or `unknown.causal.bare` (noun-only). Honest hedging: adam states what it knows about X, then explicitly says it cannot pinpoint the cause from its dataset. Closes ¬ę–Ě–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ĺ –∂–į—Ā—É—ą–į ”©–Ľ–Ķ–ī—Ė?¬Ľ which pre-v4.12.0 surfaced a generic IsA fact (logically wrong: adam asserted "X IS Y" when the user asked "WHY does X happen?"). **(3)** Backtick carve-out in `audit_response::contains_latin` ‚ÄĒ mirrors v4.7.0 corpus-purity carve-out, now applied to user-facing output. Backtick-quoted spans bypass `LatinCharactersForbidden` so technical proper nouns (`Rust`, `Cargo`, `String`, `macOS`, `Linux`, `adam-kernel`) appear verbatim; bare Latin prose outside backticks still trips the gate. **(4)** 5 new REPL replay regression dialogs (Implementation √ó 2 + Causal √ó 2 + carryover). Pipeline: 3 new template families (`ask_about_system.implementation`, `unknown.causal.with_fact`, `unknown.causal.bare`); workspace tests **749‚Üí758 passing** (+9 new: 6 question_shape + 3 backtick-audit); world_core 1 625/1 791/38 unchanged. Both v4.11.7-known gaps now answer correctly. Stripe (2) opens; v4.12.5 = discourse-acknowledgement + template rotation; v4.13.0 = graph-cohesion answer composition.

Pre-v4.11.7 the v4.11.6 length tiebreaker never fired because the priority tier already chose the scant version; now `–∂–į—Ā—É—ą–į IsA —ā—Ė—Ä—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –Ī—Ė—Ä–Ľ—Ė–≥—Ė` wins over `–∂–į—Ā—É—ą–į IsA –ľ–į—ā–Ķ—Ä–ł—Ź`. **(3)** Bare-name geo aliases (geo_kz_112..114: –∂–Ķ—ā—Ė—Ā—É, –į“õ–ľ–ĺ–Ľ–į, “Ī–Ľ—č—ā–į—É as bare-subject IsA `—ā–į—Ä–ł—Ö–ł ”©“£—Ė—Ä` / `–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā`) + `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` lowercases subject before equality so title-cased proper nouns from `normalize_proper_noun` (`“į–Ľ—č—ā–į—É`) match lowercase world_core subjects (`“Ī–Ľ—č—ā–į—É`). **(4)** Birthdate detector verb-form variants ‚ÄĒ `“õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į/–Ĺ–Ķ—ą–Ķ + –∂–į—Ā–į–Ļ—Ā—č“£/–∂–į—Ā–į–Ļ—Ā—č–∑` added alongside the existing adessive set. **(5)** Language-capability detector ‚ÄĒ closed list of {`“õ–į–∑–į“õ—ą–į / –ĺ—Ä—č—Ā—ą–į / –į“ď—č–Ľ—ą—č–Ĺ—ą–į / —ā“Į—Ä—Ė–ļ—ą–Ķ`} √ó {`–Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė“£ / –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑ / —Ā”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č“£ / —Ā”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑ / —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ė“£ / —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑`} routes to `SystemAspect::Capabilities`. Pipeline: world_core 1 622/1 785/38 ‚Üí **1 625/1 791/38**; MULTIWORD_ENTITIES +1 (`—ā–į—Ä–ł—Ö–ł ”©“£—Ė—Ä`). Workspace tests **749 passing**. **All 20 live-REPL battery queries answer correctly post-v4.11.7** (3 catastrophic + 2 partial gaps closed). **v4.11.6 ‚ÄĒ universal subject coverage patch bundle: rich-fact priority + scant cleanup + accusative fallback + adam_self subject claims + REPL baseline.** Continuation of the v4.12+ humanlike-dialog research arc. **v4.11.5 ‚ÄĒ humanlike-dialog patch bundle: 5 fixes from live REPL transcript review.** First release in the v4.12+ "human-like dialog" research arc per `project_humanlike_dialog_directive`. All 5 are catastrophic correctness failures from the 2026-04-30 transcript: ¬ę–ź–ī–į–ľ, —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ –ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ—ā—Ė“£ —Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č–Ĺ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė“£ –Ī–Ķ?¬Ľ pre-v4.11.5 returned `–į–ī–į–ľ IsA —Ā“Į—ā“õ–ĺ—Ä–Ķ–ļ—ā—Ė`; ¬ęRust —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ returned a poetry quote about the body part `—ā—Ė–Ľ`. **(1)** Vocative-addressee guard (`discourse::strip_addressee`) strips leading `–ź–ī–į–ľ, ‚Ä¶` / `–ź–ī–į–ľ! ‚Ä¶` / `–ź–ī–į–ľ —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ ‚Ä¶` BEFORE FST parsing, disambiguated from definitional `–ź–ī–į–ľ ‚ÄĒ —Ā“Į—ā“õ–ĺ—Ä–Ķ–ļ—ā—Ė.` by an addressee signal in the input. **(2)** World_core source-priority in topic extraction ‚ÄĒ `multiword_entity_hint` promoted to run BEFORE `topic_marker_hint` in `best_noun_hint`; plus inflected-form lemma fallback in `topic_marker_hint` that walks parses to find the longest noun-root which is a prefix of the inflected surface form, closing the v4.11.0 `–Ę—Ė–Ľ—Ė` fake-proper-noun bug. **(3)** Curriculum compounds in MULTIWORD_ENTITIES (+9 query-time): `—Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č`, `—Ö–ł–ľ–ł—Ź –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č`, `–Ī–ł–ĺ–Ľ–ĺ–≥–ł—Ź –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č`, `–ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ –Ņ”ô–Ĺ–ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė`, etc. **(4)** New `adam_self.jsonl` world_core domain (27 entries / 27 facts) with identity (`adam IsA —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī—Ė–ļ –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć / –ī–ł–į–Ľ–ĺ–≥ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ—Ā—Ė / –ļ–ĺ–≥–Ĺ–ł—ā–ł–≤—ā—Ė–ļ —Ź–ī—Ä–ĺ`), implementation (`adam related_to rust`, `adam IsA —Ä–Ķ—ā—Ä–ł–≤–į–Ľ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ—Ā—Ė`), per-domain knowledge claims (`adam has —Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į –Ī—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ—Ė / —Ö–ł–ľ–ł—Ź –Ī—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ—Ė / ‚Ä¶`), and curriculum-program facts (`—Ą–ł–∑–ł–ļ–į –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—Ā—č IsA –ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ –Ņ”ô–Ĺ—Ė` ‚Ä¶). 21 new compounds added to MULTIWORD_ENTITIES. `SystemIdentity::knowledge_summary` refreshed to enumerate all 38 domains. **(5)** Latin-name passthrough (`semantics::latin_subject_hint`) closes the v4.7.0 known limitation ‚ÄĒ closed list of 47 Latin-named technical subjects; when the user types one as a Latin word (case-insensitive, word-boundary-matched), it becomes the topic, so ¬ęRust —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ grounds on `\`Rust\` ‚ÄĒ –∂–į–ī—č–Ĺ—č “õ–į—É—Ė–Ņ—Ā—Ė–∑ –Ī–į—Ā“õ–į—Ä–į—ā—č–Ĺ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė` instead of poetry. Pipeline: world_core 1 593‚Üí**1 620 entries**, 1 756‚Üí**1 783 facts**, 37‚Üí**38 domains**; `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` +30 compounds; workspace 745‚Üí**749**. All 5 transcript questions land on the correct world_core fact post-v4.11.5.

**v4.11.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ `history_kazakhstan.jsonl` world_core domain (history of Kazakhstan, Kazakh).** Ninth v4.x minor; **final** in the non-Rust domain expansion track. **v4.7.21 follow-up ‚ÄĒ per-pack limit override for `rust_book_kk_pack.json`: full chapter 1‚Äď20 content now in committed morpheme_index.** Architectural follow-up to the v4.7.20 series-completion. Closes the ceiling that has carried since v4.7.7: the committed `data/retrieval/morpheme_index.json` capped each pack at `COMMITTED_DEFAULT_LIMIT = 500` samples, so chapters 8‚Äď20 (~835 sentences) were in the pack file but did not contribute to retrieval. New `PER_PACK_LIMIT_OVERRIDES` table in `build_morpheme_index.rs` registers `("rust_book_kk_pack.json", None)` ‚ÄĒ no per-pack cap. Other packs unchanged. Committed morpheme_index: 3 691 ‚Üí **4 734 indexed samples** (+1 043 ‚ÄĒ exactly the 1 543 ‚ąí 500 previously clipped); 3 362 ‚Üí **3 502 morphemes** (+140); 22 145 ‚Üí **30 919 postings** (+8 774). File size 3.9 MB (well under the 50 MB gitignore threshold). E2E threshold raised from ‚Č•490 to ‚Č•1 500. Workspace 745 unchanged.

Full Kazakh translation of Rust Book Chapter 20 ‚ÄĒ Final Project: Building a Multithreaded Web Server ‚ÄĒ the capstone chapter that ties together everything from chapters 1‚Äď19 into one real working program: a multithreaded HTTP server with graceful shutdown. Sections: building a single-threaded web server (`TcpListener`, HTTP request structure, response writing, serving HTML, request validation with `/` and `/sleep` and 404 paths); turning it multithreaded with a `ThreadPool` (compiler-driven development workflow, `mpsc::channel` + `Arc<Mutex<Receiver>>` for sharing the channel across workers, `Worker` struct with id and `JoinHandle`, the `Job = Box<dyn FnOnce() + Send + 'static>` type alias); graceful shutdown via `Drop` on `ThreadPool` (closing the channel by dropping the `sender`, joining all worker threads, the `Option::take` pattern). Pack registered in `SOURCE_PACKS` of `build_morpheme_index`, `morpheme_coverage`, `mine_lexicon_gaps`. Morpheme index: 3 082 ‚Üí **3 213 morphemes** (+131), 16 262 ‚Üí **17 637 postings** (+1 375), 3 117 ‚Üí **3 251 indexed samples** (60 chapter-1 sentences in `sample_texts`, 247 morphemes referencing rust_book samples). 1 new e2e test + 4 unit tests in the corpus binary. Workspace 740‚Üí**745**. Retrieval-ranker behaviour: world_core definitions preferred over corpus citations (correct priority); chapter sentences surface when query hits Rust-specific morpheme with no world_core match. Latin-name query limitation unchanged from v4.7.0 (deferred).

**v4.7.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ `programming_rust.jsonl` glossary + corpus-purity carve-out for technical text (phase 1 of Rust knowledge ingestion).** Fifth v4.x minor. User strategic ask: ¬ę–ĺ–Ī—É—á–ł—ā—Ć –Ĺ–į—ą—É –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć —Ź–∑—č–ļ—É –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≥—Ä–į–ľ–ľ–ł—Ä–ĺ–≤–į–Ĺ–ł—Ź Rust¬Ľ. Honest scope: adam can't generate code (retrieval-only architecture), but it CAN serve as a deterministic Kazakh-language Rust glossary ‚ÄĒ and Kazakh-language Rust documentation virtually doesn't exist outside this domain. v4.7.0 = phase 1 (curated glossary). Phases 2+ = Rust Book chapter translations as patch releases (v4.7.1, v4.7.2, ‚Ä¶). New `data/world_core/programming_rust.jsonl` carries **110 entries / 110 facts** covering Rust core (Rust, Cargo, rustc, —Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č“õ/crate, –ľ–ĺ–ī—É–Ľ—Ć), ownership / borrowing / lifetimes (–ł–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ, –ł–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ė, —Ā—Ė–Ľ—ā–Ķ–ľ–Ķ, “õ–į—Ä—č–∑“ď–į –į–Ľ—É, “õ–į—Ä—č–∑ —ā–Ķ–ļ—Ā–Ķ—Ä–≥—Ė—ą, —ā—Ė—Ä—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –ľ–Ķ—Ä–∑—Ė–ľ—Ė), variables / functions / primitive types (i32 / i64 / u32 / u64 / usize / f32 / f64 / bool / char / str / String / –ļ–ĺ—Ä—ā–Ķ–∂ / –∂–ł—č–ľ / —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ), collections (Vec / HashMap / BTreeMap / HashSet / VecDeque), structs / enums / Option / Result, control flow (if / match / loop / while / for), traits and generics (—ā—Ä–Ķ–Ļ—ā, derive, –∂–į–Ľ–Ņ—č–Ľ–į–ľ–į —ā–ł–Ņ, —ā–ł–Ņ –Ņ–į—Ä–į–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä—Ė, —ą–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ—É), error handling (panic / unwrap / expect / `?` / Drop), smart pointers / concurrency (Box / Rc / Arc / RefCell / Mutex / –į“ď—č–Ĺ / –ļ–į–Ĺ–į–Ľ / async / await / Future), iterators (map / filter / collect / –∂–į–Ī—É), unsafe blocks, modules / visibility, Cargo workflow (build / run / test / check, clippy, rustfmt). Terminology decisions locked at start of phase 1 (will guide all chapter translations in phase 2): `ownership` ‚Üí **–ł–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ**, `borrow` ‚Üí **“õ–į—Ä—č–∑“ď–į –į–Ľ—É**, `borrow checker` ‚Üí **“õ–į—Ä—č–∑ —ā–Ķ–ļ—Ā–Ķ—Ä–≥—Ė—ą**, `reference` ‚Üí **—Ā—Ė–Ľ—ā–Ķ–ľ–Ķ**, `lifetime` ‚Üí **—ā—Ė—Ä—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –ľ–Ķ—Ä–∑—Ė–ľ—Ė**, `crate` ‚Üí **—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č“õ** (preserves the wooden-crate metaphor), `trait` ‚Üí **—ā—Ä–Ķ–Ļ—ā** (transliteration), `enum/struct` ‚Üí **–Ķ–Ĺ–į–ľ/—Ā—ā—Ä—É–ļ—ā**. Code identifiers (`Vec<T>`, `Option::Some`, `match`, `let`, `fn`) are NEVER translated, kept verbatim in backticks. **Corpus-purity carve-out**: `validate_world_core::non_kazakh_reason` now skips characters inside paired backticks; bare Latin prose outside backticks is still flagged. Pipeline impact: facts.json 15 721 ‚Üí **15 831** (+110), derived 22 962 ‚Üí **23 418** (+456 via R1/R2/R5/R8 inheritance through new IsA hubs `–Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė / –ľ”ô–Ľ—Ė–ľ–Ķ—ā —ā“Į—Ä—Ė / “Ī–∂—č–ľ–ī—č“õ —ā–ł–Ņ / –Ī–į—Ā“õ–į—Ä—É “õ“Ī—Ä—č–Ľ—č–ľ—č / –∂–į–ī –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ė / —ā—Ä–Ķ–Ļ—ā`), MULTIWORD_ENTITIES +52 compounds, lexicon +24 noun roots. **Known limitations** (resolved in later phases): direct Latin-name queries (¬ęRust –ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė–ľ—Ė–∑ –Ĺ–Ķ?¬Ľ, ¬ęCargo –ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė–ľ—Ė–∑ –Ĺ–Ķ?¬Ľ) don't tokenize through the Cyrillic-only FST and fall through to Unknown; Kazakh-paraphrased queries (–ė–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ļ / –Ę—Ä–Ķ–Ļ—ā / –°—Ė–Ľ—ā–Ķ–ľ–Ķ / –Ę—Ė—Ä—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –ľ–Ķ—Ä–∑—Ė–ľ—Ė) work correctly. ASCII-identifier passthrough is deferred to a later patch once Rust Book chapter content surfaces enough Latin-prose context to justify it. No code generation ‚ÄĒ retrieval-only architecture stands. World Core 1032/1195/32‚Üí**1142/1305/33**, REPL replay 68/68‚Üí**69/69**, workspace 739‚Üí**740**. Why minor: new world_core domain shipping with the corpus-purity rule (architectural carve-out) + 24-root lexicon expansion + 52-compound MULTIWORD_ENTITIES growth + 110-fact knowledge base.

**v4.6.20 follow-up ‚ÄĒ 5 more innovations bundled (20 total cumulative on the v4.6.x minor): reflexive identity question + adj+noun compound noun-hint + `SelfComparison` aspect + discourse-preamble stripper + `UserAcknowledgement` intent.** Real-REPL 2026-04-29 (fifth transcript) surfaced 5 distinct defects sharing one theme: adam couldn't make sense of long, multi-clause Kazakh sentences ‚ÄĒ greedy noun-hint extraction grabbed adverbs (`”ô–Ľ—Ė`) or modifier-stripped head nouns (`–ĺ“õ—č—ā—É` from ¬ę–ľ–į—ą–ł–Ĺ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ĺ“õ—č—ā—É¬Ľ), then surfaced random poetry/contract quotes. **(1)** `detect_ask_about_system` extended for reflexive identity questions ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –ļ—Ė–ľ –ī–Ķ–Ņ —Ā–į–Ĺ–į–Ļ—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ / ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£–ī—Ė “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ —ā–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č—Ä–į—Ā—č“£?¬Ľ (marker: `”©–∑—Ė“£–ī—Ė / ”©–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė` + 2nd-person verb), routed to `SystemAspect::General`. **(2)** New `discourse::find_adj_noun_compound` returns the longest matching closed-list compound (`–ľ–į—ą–ł–Ĺ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ĺ“õ—č—ā—É`, `–∂–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č –ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā`, `—ā–į–Ī–ł“ď–ł —ā—Ė–Ľ`, `—ā–Ķ—Ä–Ķ“£ –ĺ“õ—č—ā—É`, `–Ĺ–Ķ–Ļ—Ä–ĺ–Ĺ–ī—č“õ –∂–Ķ–Ľ—Ė` ‚Ä¶) found in input ‚ÄĒ wired as the FIRST strategy in `best_noun_hint`. **(3)** New `SystemAspect::SelfComparison` (9th variant) + `system_self_comparison` slot + `ask_about_system.self_comparison` template family. Detector pairs comparison marker (`–į—Ä—ā—č“õ / –∂–į“õ—Ā—č—Ä–į“õ / –ĺ–∑–į—Ā—č“£`) with addressee marker including the `-—Ā—č“£/-—Ā—č–∑` ability suffix; honest framing ‚ÄĒ adam articulates the trade-off (narrow Kazakh-only competence with strong invariants vs. broad LLM coverage), not superiority. Closes ¬ę–Ď–į—Ā“õ–į –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–ī–Ķ—Ä–ī–Ķ–Ĺ –Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –į—Ä—ā—č“õ—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ, ¬ę“ö–ĺ–Ľ–ī–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā–į“ď—č –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–ī–Ķ—Ä–ī–Ķ–Ĺ “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –∂–į“õ—Ā—č—Ä–į“õ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ. **(4)** New `discourse::strip_preamble` runs at the top of `Conversation::turn_with_trace` BEFORE FST parsing. Closed list of 24 leading preambles (`–į–Ļ—ā–į–Ļ—č–Ĺ –ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė–ľ`, `“õ—č—Ā“õ–į—ą–į –į–Ļ—ā“õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į`, `—ą—č–Ĺ—č–Ĺ–ī–į`, `—Ā“Ī—Ä–į“ď—č–ľ –ľ—č–Ĺ–į—É`, `–∂–į–Ľ–Ņ—č –į–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ–ī–į`, `–į–Ļ—ā–Ņ–į“õ—ą—č` ‚Ä¶); when matched at input start with a clause separator after, the preamble is removed and the residual goes to the parser. Russian/math/anaphor detection still see the raw input. **(5)** New `Intent::UserAcknowledgement` (27th variant) + `user_acknowledgement` template family. Detector: addressee marker + 1sg perfective realisation verb (`—ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ľ / –Ī—Ė–Ľ–ī—Ė–ľ / –ļ”©—Ä–ī—Ė–ľ / –Ī–į–Ļ“õ–į–ī—č–ľ / “Ī“õ—ā—č–ľ / –į“£“ď–į—Ä–ī—č–ľ / —Ā–Ķ–∑—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ľ`) + not-a-question. Polite acknowledgement reply (¬ę—Ä–į—Ö–ľ–Ķ—ā, —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£—Ė–∑–≥–Ķ “õ—É–į–Ĺ—č—ą—ā—č–ľ—č–Ĺ. –ú–Ķ–Ĺ ”ô–Ľ—Ė –ī–į–ľ—č–Ņ –ļ–Ķ–Ľ–Ķ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ ‚Ä¶¬Ľ). Closes ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ ”ô–Ľ—Ė –Ī”ô—Ä—Ė–Ĺ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ—ā—Ė–Ĺ—Ė“£–ī—Ė ‚Ä¶ —ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–ī—Ė–ľ¬Ľ. 5 new e2e + 5 new REPL replay dialogs. `discourse.rs` helpers 3‚Üí**7**, SystemAspect variants 8‚Üí**9**, Intent variants 26‚Üí**27**, template families 57‚Üí**59**, REPL replay 63/63‚Üí**68/68**, workspace 734‚Üí**739**.

**v4.6.15 follow-up ‚ÄĒ 3 more innovations bundled (15 total cumulative on the v4.6.x minor): integer arithmetic calculator + `mathematics_basic` world_core domain + `informatics_basic` world_core domain.** User strategic ask: ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ–ĺ–Ī—Ö–ĺ–ī–ł–ľ–ĺ –ī–į—ā—Ć –Ķ–ľ—É –∑–Ĺ–į–Ĺ–ł—Ź —ą–ļ–ĺ–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ–ĺ–Ļ –Ņ—Ä–ĺ–≥—Ä–į–ľ–ľ—č –Ņ–ĺ –ľ–į—ā–Ķ–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–Ķ –ł –ł–Ĺ—Ą–ĺ—Ä–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–Ķ ‚Ä¶ –ě–Ĺ –ī–ĺ–Ľ–∂–Ķ–Ĺ –Ņ–ĺ–Ĺ–ł–ľ–į—ā—Ć –ī–ł–į–Ľ–ĺ–≥, —ā–ĺ–≥–ĺ, —á—ā–ĺ –ĺ—ā –Ĺ–Ķ–≥–ĺ —Ö–ĺ—ā—Ź—ā¬Ľ. v4.6.12 detected math expressions and refused; v4.6.15 evaluates them deterministically and adds two new world_core domains so adam knows what the school terms *mean*. **(1)** New `discourse::try_evaluate_arithmetic` deterministic two-pass tokeniser/evaluator over `+ ‚ąí √ó √∑ :` (`:` normalised to `/`), respects precedence, rejects non-integer results / division-by-zero / overflow. The conversation layer first attempts evaluation when the v4.6.12 math detector fires; on success the planner routes to a new `math_answer` template family. Closes from real-REPL: ¬ę5+5 ‚Üí 10¬Ľ, ¬ę6:2= ‚Üí 3¬Ľ, ¬ę12*4 ‚Üí 48¬Ľ, ¬ę2+3*4 ‚Üí 14¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ pure stdlib `i64`, no external numeric library. **(2)** `mathematics_basic.jsonl` (37 entries / 37 facts): –ľ–į—ā–Ķ–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–į, —Ā–į–Ĺ, –į–ľ–į–Ľ, “õ–ĺ—Ā—É/–į–∑–į–Ļ—ā—É/–ļ”©–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—ā—É/–Ī”©–Ľ—É, —ā–Ķ“£–ī—Ė–ļ, —ā–Ķ“£–ī–Ķ—É, –Ī”©–Ľ—ą–Ķ–ļ, –Ņ–į–Ļ—č–∑, –į–Ľ–≥–Ķ–Ī—Ä–į/–≥–Ķ–ĺ–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä–ł—Ź/—ā—Ä–ł–≥–ĺ–Ĺ–ĺ–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä–ł—Ź, —Ą–ł–≥—É—Ä–į, –Ĺ“Į–ļ—ā–Ķ, —ā“Į–∑—É, –Ī“Ī—Ä—č—ą, —ą–Ķ“£–Ī–Ķ—Ä, –ī”©“£–≥–Ķ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ, “Į—ą–Ī“Ī—Ä—č—ą/—ā”©—Ä—ā–Ī“Ī—Ä—č—ą/—ą–į—Ä—ą—č/—ā—Ė–ļ—ā”©—Ä—ā–Ī“Ī—Ä—č—ą/–ļ”©–Ņ–Ī“Ī—Ä—č—ą, –∂“Ī–Ņ/—ā–į“õ/–∂–į–Ļ/–Ī“Į—ā—Ė–Ĺ/–Ĺ–į—ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ —Ā–į–Ĺ, –ļ”©–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—ā—É –ļ–Ķ—Ā—ā–Ķ—Ā—Ė, –į—É–ī–į–Ĺ/–ļ”©–Ľ–Ķ–ľ/–Ņ–Ķ—Ä–ł–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä, —ą–į–ľ–į, —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź. **(3)** `informatics_basic.jsonl` (40 entries / 40 facts): –ł–Ĺ—Ą–ĺ—Ä–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–į, –į“õ–Ņ–į—Ä–į—ā, –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ, –į–Ľ–≥–ĺ—Ä–ł—ā–ľ, –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į, –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į–Ľ–į—É —ā—Ė–Ľ—Ė, –ļ–ĺ–ľ–Ņ—Ć—é—ā–Ķ—Ä, –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ü–Ķ—Ā—Ā–ĺ—Ä, –∂–į–ī, —Ą–į–Ļ–Ľ, –Ī–ł—ā/–Ī–į–Ļ—ā, –į–Ļ–Ĺ—č–ľ–į–Ľ—č/—ā“Ī—Ä–į“õ—ā—č, —Ü–ł–ļ–Ľ/—ą–į—Ä—ā/—Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź/–∂–ł—č–ľ, –ī–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ—Ä –Ī–į–∑–į—Ā—č, –∂–Ķ–Ľ—Ė/–ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ—Ä–Ĺ–Ķ—ā/—Ā–į–Ļ—ā/—ą–ĺ–Ľ“ď—č—ą/—Ā–Ķ—Ä–≤–Ķ—Ä, –ļ–ĺ–ī—ā–į—É/—ą–ł—Ą—Ä–Ľ–į—É/–Ņ–į—Ä–ĺ–Ľ—Ć, –≤–ł—Ä—É—Ā/–į–Ĺ—ā–ł–≤–ł—Ä—É—Ā, –ĺ–Ņ–Ķ—Ä–į—Ü–ł—Ź–Ľ—č“õ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ, –ī—Ä–į–Ļ–≤–Ķ—Ä, “õ–ĺ–Ľ–ī–į–Ĺ–Ī–į, –Ņ–Ķ—Ä–Ĺ–Ķ—ā–į“õ—ā–į/—ā—Ė–Ĺ—ā—É—Ė—Ä/–ľ–ĺ–Ĺ–ł—ā–ĺ—Ä/–Ņ—Ä–ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ—Ä/—Ā–ļ–į–Ĺ–Ķ—Ä. **v4.6.12 follow-up ‚ÄĒ 7 more innovations bundled (12 total cumulative on the v4.6.x minor).** Real-REPL 2026-04-29 (third transcript) surfaced 7 distinct issues. **(1)** AskHowAreYou +polite-plural ¬ę“ö–į–Ľ—č“£—č–∑ “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ?¬Ľ. **(2)** Fix `greeting.intro_proposal` template grammar ‚ÄĒ pre-v4.6.12 4th variant said ¬ę—Ā—Ė–∑ “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ —ā–į–Ĺ—č—Ā–į–ľ—č–∑?¬Ľ (2sg-polite + 1pl-future, ungrammatical), replaced with ¬ę—Ā—Ė–∑–ī—Ė “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –į—ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ?¬Ľ. **(3)** Russian-input refusal ‚ÄĒ new `discourse::input_is_likely_russian` detector + `__non_kazakh__` marker + `unknown.non_kazakh` template family. Closes ¬ę5+5¬Ľ, ¬ę6:2=¬Ľ, ¬ę5-—ā—Ė 7-–≥–Ķ –ļ”©–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—ā–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ–ī–Ķ¬Ľ, ¬ę–į–Ľ—ā—č–Ĺ—č –Ķ–ļ—Ė–≥–Ķ –Ī”©–Ľ—Ė“£—Ė–∑¬Ľ (last one also resolves the –į–Ľ—ā—č/–į–Ľ—ā—č–Ĺ homonym ambiguity by short-circuiting before topic extraction). **(7)** Closed-class case-suffix hygiene ‚ÄĒ bare suffixes `–≥–Ķ / –ļ–Ķ / –ī–Ķ / —ā–Ķ / –ī–į / —ā–į / –Ī–Ķ / –ľ–į` added to NOT_A_TOPIC. **v4.6.5 follow-up ‚ÄĒ 5 innovations bundled: Creator detector +3 verbs + capitalization + period gate + Principles aspect + forbidden-pattern filter.** Real-REPL 2026-04-29 (second transcript) surfaced a new defect class + the user requested orthographic + value-articulation layers. **(1) Creator detector** extended with `–∂–į—Ä–į—ā—ā—č` / `–ī–į–ľ—č—ā“õ–į–Ĺ` / `–ī–į–ľ—č—ā—ā—č` / `–ī–į–Ļ—č–Ĺ–ī–į–ī—č` / `–∂–į—Ä–į—ā—É—ą—č“£` / `“õ–į–Ļ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č` patterns ‚ÄĒ pre-v4.6.5 ¬ę–ź–Ľ —Ā–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė –ļ—Ė–ľ –∂–į—Ä–į—ā—ā—č?¬Ľ / ¬ę–°—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –ļ—Ė–ľ –ī–į–ľ—č—ā“õ–į–Ĺ?¬Ľ / ¬ę–°—Ė–∑–ī—Ė “õ–į–Ļ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č –ī–į–Ļ—č–Ĺ–ī–į–ī—č?¬Ľ all fell through to refusal. **(2) Capitalization** ‚ÄĒ every reply now starts with an uppercase letter (sentence-case). New `capitalise_first_letter` orthographic pass in `realiser::realise` past leading whitespace/punctuation; Cyrillic-Kazakh-aware via `char::to_uppercase`. **(3) Sentence-final period** ‚ÄĒ declarative replies ‚Č•10 codepoints ending in an alphabetic character now get `.` appended. Short interjections (¬ę–°”ô–Ľ–Ķ–ľ¬Ľ, ¬ę–ė”ô¬Ľ) stay as-is. **(4) `SystemAspect::Principles`** ‚ÄĒ new variant + `principles_summary` field on `SystemIdentity` listing operational values adam upholds: respect humans, no fabrication, no incitement, privacy, no illegal-act assistance, audit trail, Kazakh-cultural respect, scope discipline. New `ask_about_system.principles` template family + detector for `–Ņ—Ä–ł–Ĺ—Ü–ł–Ņ—ā–Ķ—Ä—Ė“£ / “Ī—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ—č–ľ–ī–į—Ä—č“£ / –∑–į“£–ī–į—Ä—č“£ / –Ķ—Ä–Ķ–∂–Ķ–Ľ–Ķ—Ä—Ė“£ / “õ“Ī–Ĺ–ī—č–Ľ—č“õ—ā–į—Ä—č“£`. Articulation layer ‚ÄĒ the underlying guarantees are already safe-by-construction. **(5) Forbidden-pattern filter** ‚ÄĒ new `ResponseQualityIssue::ForbiddenPatternLeak` defensive backstop in `audit_response`. Catches a regression that bypasses curation; not the primary safety mechanism (adam's retrieval-only design keeps that at the curation layer). Workspace **703 ‚Üí 715**, cognitive **63/63 ‚Üí 65/65**, REPL replay **50/50 ‚Üí 55/55**, template families **53 ‚Üí 54**, `SystemAspect` variants **7 ‚Üí 8**.

**v4.6.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ self-awareness layer + discourse anaphora + closed-class hygiene.** Fourth v4.x minor. Real-REPL 2026-04-29 transcript surfaced 6 distinct defects + a strategic ask for self-awareness. All landed in one release. **(1) Self-awareness ‚ÄĒ three new SystemAspect variants** (`Capabilities`, `Knowledge`, `Limitations`) with corresponding template families (`ask_about_system.capabilities` / `.knowledge` / `.limitations`) and three new `SystemIdentity` summary fields rendered as honest, grounded Kazakh prose: ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ —Ė—Ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č“£?¬Ľ ‚Üí adam lists what it can do (KZ morphology, slot recall, KZ geography knowledge, contradiction handling, audit trail); ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė“£?¬Ľ ‚Üí adam lists its world_core knowledge domains; ¬ę–Ĺ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė —Ė—Ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ –į–Ľ–ľ–į–Ļ—Ā—č“£?¬Ľ ‚Üí adam states its limitations (Kazakh-only, no novel generation, no online learning, no internet, no multimedia, no math). The Limitations detector is gated on an explicit interrogative marker so declarative criticism ¬ę—Ā–Ķ–Ĺ –Ķ—ą—ā–Ķ“£–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ—Ā—Ė“£¬Ľ does NOT route here (preserves the v4.4.10 `qysqasy_discourse_particle` Tentative floor). **(2) Discourse anaphora** ‚ÄĒ new `crates/adam-dialog/src/discourse.rs` module + `last_query_topic` session slot. When the user's input contains a discourse anaphor (¬ę–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į / —Ā–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į / –ĺ—Ā—č–Ĺ–ī–į / –ľ“Ī–Ĺ–ī–į / –Ī“Ī–Ĺ–ī–į / –ĺ–ī–į–Ĺ / —Ā–ĺ–ī–į–Ĺ / –Ī“Ī–ī–į–Ĺ / –ĺ—Ā—č–ī–į–Ĺ¬Ľ), the conversation layer **overrides** the current turn's `noun_hint` with the previous turn's topic. So ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ĺ–Ķ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑?¬Ľ ‚Üí ¬ę–ź–Ľ –ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į –į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ –Ī–į—Ä?¬Ľ now answers with ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–Ĺ—č“£ –į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ—ā–į—Ä—č ‚ÄĒ 17 –ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā –Ņ–Ķ–Ĺ 3 —Ä–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—É–Ī–Ľ–ł–ļ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ľ–į“£—č–∑—č –Ī–į—Ä “õ–į–Ľ–į¬Ľ instead of ¬ę–ě–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ —Ā–į–Ĺ¬Ľ. **(3) Compound self-introduction** ‚ÄĒ extended `detect_ask_about_system` to fire on `”©–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –į–Ļ—ā` openers (real-REPL ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –į–Ļ—ā—č–Ņ –Ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė“£—Ė–∑—ą—Ė¬Ľ). **(4) Closed-class hygiene** ‚ÄĒ added `”©—ā–Ķ` (intensifier "very") and `–∂–į–Ľ–Ņ—č` (in-general adverb) to NOT_A_TOPIC; added bare numeral roots `–ĺ–Ĺ` / `—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ` to filter the FST misanalysis of `–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į / —Ā–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į` as `Locative(–ĺ–Ĺ/—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ)`. **(5) New world_core landmarks fact** ‚ÄĒ ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č –ļ”©—Ä—Ė–ļ—ā—Ė –∂–Ķ—Ä–Ľ–Ķ—Ä –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ —ā–į–Ī–ł“ď–ł –ĺ—Ä—č–Ĺ–ī–į—Ä: –Ď—É—Ä–į–Ī–į–Ļ, –®–į—Ä—č–Ĺ –ļ–į–Ĺ—Ć–ĺ–Ĺ—č, –•–į–Ĺ –Ę”ô“£—Ė—Ä—Ė, ‚Ä¶¬Ľ surfaced when user asks ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –ļ”©—Ä—Ė–ļ—ā—Ė –∂–Ķ—Ä–Ľ–Ķ—Ä –Ī–į—Ä?¬Ľ. World Core **947 ‚Üí 949 entries / 1116 ‚Üí 1120 facts** (+1 landmarks list + 1 area-quantity fact). Cognitive eval **59/59 ‚Üí 63/63**, REPL replay **43/43 ‚Üí 50/50**, workspace **693 ‚Üí 703**. Why minor: 3 new SystemAspect enum variants + 1 new module (`discourse.rs`) + 1 new session-state slot ‚ÄĒ multiple architectural type-system additions.

**v4.5.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ `Case::LocativeAttributive` FST morphotactics rule.** Closes the v4.4.12/13 carry-forward by replacing the v4.4.12 string-side fallback with a proper morphotactics rule. New `Case::LocativeAttributive` enum variant in `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/morphotactics.rs` + new `LOCATIVE_ATTRIBUTIVE` suffix template `-{D}{A}{G}{I}` covering all four allomorphs (`-–ī–į“ď—č` back-voiced, `-–ī–Ķ–≥—Ė` front-voiced, `-—ā–į“ď—č` back-voiceless, `-—ā–Ķ–≥—Ė` front-voiceless) via the existing archiphoneme machinery. Pronominal-–Ĺ buffer rule extended to apply on P3 + LocativeAttributive. The parser's `try_noun_analyses` enumerates the new case, so analyse() reverse-parses surface forms back to the base noun. **Full round-trip verified**: `synthesise(“õ–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ, LocativeAttributive)` ‚Üí `“õ–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č`; `analyse(“õ–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č)` ‚Üí `Noun(“õ–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ, LocativeAttributive)`. CLI gained `--case locattr`. The v4.4.12 string-side `locative_attributive_hint` stays in place as a backstop for stems whose base form isn't yet in the lexicon. Why minor: new code-level Case variant + new morphotactics rule + round-trip synthesis support ‚ÄĒ architectural addition by the post-1.0 cadence rule. Workspace **692 ‚Üí 693**.

**v4.4.13 follow-up ‚ÄĒ lexicon hygiene patch.** Two long-standing FST/lexicon defects, surfaced during the v4.4.12 trace and queued at the time. **(1) Multi-POS homonym dedup.** `Lexicon::load` deduplicated by surface root via a `HashMap<String, RootEntry>`, so multi-POS homonyms like `—ā–į—É` (verb_tau + noun_apt_tau, both keyed on the same surface) silently lost one reading and only the last-inserted one survived in `entries_ordered` ‚ÄĒ the FST analyser's iteration source. Result: `—ā–į—É` parsed only as a verb root, never as the noun "mountain". **Fix**: separate `entries_ordered` (full union of both lexicon files, deduplicated only by `id` to handle exact-copy entries) from `by_surface` (intentionally lossy single-POS lookup table for downstream code that doesn't care about POS). **(2) Missing core nouns.** Audit found `—Ā—É` (water), `–ĺ—ā` (fire), `–Ķ—Ä` (saddle / man-as-hero) absent from both lexicon files entirely. Added to `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json`. **(3) `best_noun_hint` chain reorder** ‚ÄĒ `locative_attributive_hint` was running AFTER `first_noun_root` (correct as a fallback in v4.4.12), but v4.4.13's lexicon-dedup fix unblocked content nouns like `—ā–į—É` so `first_noun_root` started masking the locative-attributive signal on questions like `“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?`. Reordered so locative-attributive runs first ‚ÄĒ `-–ī–į“ď—č` is a strong topic-narrowing signal semantically equivalent to a `—ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č` marker for the word it attaches to. All 5 listing-style questions now answer correctly with both locative (`“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä –Ī–į—Ä?`) and locative-attributive (`“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?`) phrasings. Cognitive **59/59 ‚Üí 59/59** (no scenario added ‚ÄĒ the locking is at REPL replay layer), REPL replay **40/40 ‚Üí 43/43** (+3 listing-via-locative-attributive dialogs), workspace **690 ‚Üí 692** (+2 lexicon e2e).

**v4.4.12 follow-up ‚ÄĒ locative-attributive `-–ī–į“ď—č / -–ī–Ķ–≥—Ė / -—ā–į“ď—č / -—ā–Ķ–≥—Ė` suffix recovery.** Closes the v4.4.11 carry-forward where `“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?` fell through to the generic refusal because the FST morphotactics has no rule for the locative-attributive derivation (Kazakh forms ¬ęlocated in X¬Ľ attributives by attaching `-“ď—č / -–≥—Ė / -“õ—č / -–ļ—Ė` to the locative-cased stem). The FST returns no analysis for `“õ–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č`, so `best_noun_hint` recovered nothing. v4.4.12 added a string-level `locative_attributive_hint` fallback in `crates/adam-dialog/src/semantics.rs` that scans tokens for the four allomorphs, strips the 4-char tail, and recovers the base noun (‚Č• 3 codepoints, not in NOT_A_TOPIC). Combined with v4.4.11's input-overlap reranker the question now answers with the literal mountains list. The fallback is conservative ‚ÄĒ promoted to a proper `Case::LocativeAttributive` morphotactics rule in a future minor. Cognitive **58/58 ‚Üí 59/59**, REPL replay **39/39 ‚Üí 40/40**, workspace **688 ‚Üí 690**.

**v4.4.11 follow-up ‚ÄĒ input-overlap retrieval reranker + list-summary renderer fix.** Closes the v4.4.10 carry-forward where listing-style questions (¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ –į–Ļ–ľ–į“õ—ā–į—Ä—č–Ĺ—č“£ –į—ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä—č–Ĺ –Ī—Ė–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–∑ –Ī–Ķ?¬Ľ, ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –ļ”©–Ľ–ī–Ķ—Ä –Ī–į—Ä?¬Ľ) retrieved the most-central ¬ę“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ –ě—Ä—ā–į–Ľ—č“õ –ź–∑–ł—Ź–ī–į“ď—č –Ķ–Ľ¬Ľ IsA fact instead of the specific list-summary entries. Two-part fix: (1) **input-morpheme-overlap reranker** in `Tool::dispatch(SearchGraph)` ‚ÄĒ `ToolContext` gained a `query_input: Option<&str>` field which the rank function uses to score each fact's `raw_text` against the user's content tokens (4-char prefix substring match handles agglutinative inflection); higher overlap wins, ties fall through to the v4.0.x predicate-rank tier (IsA ‚Üí LivesIn ‚Üí HasQuantity ‚Üí ‚Ä¶). (2) **list-summary RelatedTo renderer** in `tool.rs::render_grounded_fact` ‚ÄĒ when the fact's object root contains ¬ę—ā—Ė–∑—Ė–ľ¬Ľ, surface `raw_text` directly instead of the generic ¬ęX –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ Y ”©–∑–į—Ä–į –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č¬Ľ template. All 5 v4.4.10 carry-forward listing questions now answer with literal lists: aliases / lakes / rivers / mountains / deserts. Cognitive **57/57 ‚Üí 58/58**, REPL replay **35/35 ‚Üí 39/39**, workspace **687 ‚Üí 688**.

**v4.4.10 follow-up ‚ÄĒ Kazakhstan administrative + physical geography expansion + `–Ę–į–Ĺ—č—Ā–į–Ļ—č“õ` intent + `“ö—č—Ā“õ–į—Ā—č` topic-marker guard.** Real-REPL transcript on 2026-04-28 surfaced 5 distinct issues. Three knowledge gaps fixed by authoring **76 new world_core entries** in `data/world_core/geography_kz.jsonl` (873 ‚Üí **947 entries**, 995 ‚Üí **1116 facts**, 21 415 ‚Üí **22 387 derivations** from new `”©–∑–Ķ–Ĺ/–ļ”©–Ľ/—ā–Ķ“£—Ė–∑ IsA —Ā—É –ī–Ķ–Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ė`, `—ā–į—É/—ą”©–Ľ/–ļ–į–Ĺ—Ć–ĺ–Ĺ IsA –∂–Ķ—Ä –Ī–Ķ–ī–Ķ—Ä—Ė`, `–ĺ–Ī–Ľ—č—Ā IsA ”ô–ļ—Ė–ľ—ą—Ė–Ľ—Ė–ļ –Ī”©–Ľ—Ė–ļ`, `“õ–į–Ľ–į/–į—É—č–Ľ IsA –Ķ–Ľ–ī—Ė –ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ` bridge facts): all **17 Kazakh oblasts** as administrative entities (`–ź–Ī–į–Ļ`, `–ź“õ–ľ–ĺ–Ľ–į`, `–ź“õ—ā”©–Ī–Ķ`, `–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č`, `–ź—ā—č—Ä–į—É`, `–Ď–į—ā—č—Ā “ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ`, `–Ė–į–ľ–Ī—č–Ľ`, `–Ė–Ķ—ā—Ė—Ā—É`, `“ö–į—Ä–į“ď–į–Ĺ–ī—č`, `“ö–ĺ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–į–Ļ`, `“ö—č–∑—č–Ľ–ĺ—Ä–ī–į`, `–ú–į“£“ď—č—Ā—ā–į—É`, `–ü–į–≤–Ľ–ĺ–ī–į—Ä`, `–°–ĺ–Ľ—ā“Į—Ā—ā—Ė–ļ “ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ`, `–Ę“Į—Ä–ļ—Ė—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ`, `“į–Ľ—č—ā–į—É`, `–®—č“ď—č—Ā “ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ`), oblast ‚Üí administrative-center mappings (–°–Ķ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ‚Üí–ź–Ī–į–Ļ, –ö”©–ļ—ą–Ķ—ā–į—É‚Üí–ź“õ–ľ–ĺ–Ľ–į, ‚Ä¶, “ö–ĺ–Ĺ–į–Ķ–≤‚Üí–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č (post-2022 reform), –ü–Ķ—ā—Ä–ĺ–Ņ–į–≤–Ľ‚Üí–°“ö–ě, –Ė–Ķ–∑“õ–į–∑“ď–į–Ĺ‚Üí“į–Ľ—č—ā–į—É, –Ę“Į—Ä–ļ—Ė—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ‚Üí–Ę“Į—Ä–ļ—Ė—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ oblast), 3 cities of republican significance upgrade (–ź—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–į / –ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č / –®—č–ľ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—ā `IsA —Ä–Ķ—Ā–Ņ—É–Ī–Ľ–ł–ļ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ľ–į“£—č–∑—č –Ī–į—Ä “õ–į–Ľ–į`), country + 3-republic-city population facts (~20 / ~2 / ~1.5 / ~1.2 –ľ–Ľ–Ĺ), 6 new rivers (`–Ė–į–Ļ—č“õ`, `–ē—Ā—Ė–Ľ`, `–Ę–ĺ–Ī—č–Ľ`, `–®—É`, `“ö–į—Ä–į—ā–į–Ľ`, `–Ę–į–Ľ–į—Ā`), 4 new lakes (`–ó–į–Ļ—Ā–į–Ĺ`, `–ź–Ľ–į–ļ”©–Ľ`, `–Ę–Ķ–Ĺ–≥—Ė–∑`, `–ú–į—Ä–ļ–į–ļ”©–Ľ`), 5 mountains (`–Ę—Ź–Ĺ—Ć-–®–į–Ĺ—Ć`, `–Ė–Ķ—ā—Ė—Ā—É –ź–Ľ–į—ā–į—É—č`, `–•–į–Ĺ –Ę”ô“£—Ė—Ä—Ė`, `“ö–į—Ä–į—ā–į—É`, `“į–Ľ—č—ā–į—É`), 4 deserts (`–Ď–Ķ—ā–Ņ–į“õ–ī–į–Ľ–į`, `“ö—č–∑—č–Ľ“õ“Ī–ľ`, `“ģ—Ā—ā—Ė—Ä—ā`, `–ú–ĺ–Ļ—č–Ĺ“õ“Ī–ľ`), `–®–į—Ä—č–Ĺ –ļ–į–Ĺ—Ć–ĺ–Ĺ—č`, `–Ď—É—Ä–į–Ī–į–Ļ`. Two dialog issues: new `GreetingKind::IntroProposal` + `greeting.intro_proposal` template family routes `–Ę–į–Ĺ—č—Ā–į–Ļ—č“õ` to a self-introduction reply (was falling through to safe-fallback refusal); NOT_A_TOPIC additions for `“õ—č—Ā“õ–į` / `–Ķ—ą—ā–Ķ“£–Ķ` / `–Ķ—ą–ļ—Ė–ľ` / `–Ķ—ą–Ī—Ė—Ä` / `–Ķ—ą` close the discourse-particle / quantifier-pronoun topic-extraction misfires. Cognitive eval **55/55 ‚Üí 57/57**, REPL replay **31/31 ‚Üí 35/35**, workspace **683 ‚Üí 687**. **v4.4.9 follow-up ‚ÄĒ AskName 1sg self-recall + slot-echo aspirationals promoted.** (1) `–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –į—ā—č–ľ –ļ—Ė–ľ?` after `–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –į—ā—č–ľ –Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā` was misclassified as `StatementOfName { name: "–ö—Ė–ľ" }` pre-v4.4.9 ‚ÄĒ `detect_statement_of_name`'s "–į—ā—č–ľ X" pattern blindly grabbed the question word `–ö—Ė–ľ` as a name, then logged a phantom `BeliefConflict` (–Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā vs –ö—Ė–ľ) and emitted a clarifying question naming both. Symmetric to v4.4.5 / v4.4.6 self-recall fixes but worse: belief got mutated, not just surface text. Fix: interrogative-pronoun guard in `detect_statement_of_name` (refuses `–ļ—Ė–ľ / –Ĺ–Ķ / “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ / “õ–į–Ļ—Ā—č—Ā—č` across all three patterns) + extended `detect_ask_name` (accepts 1sg `–į—ā—č–ľ / –Ķ—Ā—Ė–ľ—Ė–ľ + –ļ—Ė–ľ / –Ĺ–Ķ`). The REPL replay battery surfaced this on v4.4.6 first run. (2) Promoted all 3 aspirational REPL replay dialogs (`city_statement_acknowledged`, `age_statement_acknowledged`, `occupation_statement_acknowledged`) to canonical by rewriting the 5 bare variants in `statement_of_*` template families to interpolate their slot. REPL replay baseline 27/27 + 3 ‚Üí **31/31 + 0 aspirational**, cognitive eval 54/54 ‚Üí **55/55**, workspace 681 ‚Üí 683. Performance regression policy clarified: thermal throttling on the M2 8 GB can uniformly elevate p50 by ~70 % under sustained `cargo` load; comparison must be apples-to-apples on thermal state (proven environmental in v4.4.9 via stash-and-re-bench).

**v4.4.7 follow-up ‚ÄĒ performance baseline.** Per-turn latency, cold-start cost, and RSS measured on M2 8 GB: **p50 1.07 ms** (`—Ā”ô–Ľ–Ķ–ľ`) ‚Üí **6.04 ms** (3-turn dismiss-contradiction dialog), cold start **~14 ms**, max RSS **~76‚Äď80 MB** depending on the metric (`/usr/bin/time -l` reports `maximum resident set size` ‚Čą 80 MB and `peak memory footprint` ‚Čą 76 MB on the same run). Honest "when adam, when LLM" comparison block: latency / memory delta is 100√ó‚Äď2 000√ó vs a local LLM, but only meaningful **inside adam's competence envelope** ‚ÄĒ Kazakh dialog intents recognised by the recogniser, slots filled from FST parses or curated entities, knowledge queries that hit `world_core` or the retrieval shards. Outside that envelope adam refuses or admits uncertainty; it does not fabricate. Numbers and methodology in [docs/performance.md](docs/performance.md); reproduce with `cargo bench -p adam-dialog --bench turn_latency`. Performance regressions > 20 % p50 are release blockers per [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md).

**v4.4.6 follow-up ‚ÄĒ REPL replay battery + AskOccupation 1sg self-recall.** New `crates/adam-dialog/tests/repl_replay.rs` harness running `data/eval/repl_dialogs.json` (30 hand-authored multi-turn KZ dialogs) ‚ÄĒ complementary to `cognitive_eval` (which checks trace signals); this checks what the user actually sees. Same `expected_failing` aspirational contract. Current baseline **27/27 canonical + 3 aspirational** (the 3 aspirational document a real `statement_of_*` slot-echo gap; promotion-ready when every variant interpolates the slot). Plus a v4.4.5-class detector extension surfaced by the harness on first run: `–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –ľ–į–ľ–į–Ĺ–ī—č“ď—č–ľ –Ĺ–Ķ?` now classifies as `AskOccupation` and recalls the stored value via `ask_occupation.with_known_user`. New `CONTRIBUTING.md` codifies the load-bearing rule that's been informal for several releases ‚ÄĒ every dialog defect ships with at least one new scenario / dialog.

**v4.4.5 follow-up ‚ÄĒ real-dialog adequacy fixes.** External review (Codex, 2026-04-27 live REPL) caught two user-visible defects the internal suite missed: (1) `Action::CheckContradiction` rendered as a confirmation because the planner kept keying on `intent_key(intent)` instead of the action ‚ÄĒ answer was ¬ę–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ī–į –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –Ķ—Ā—ā–Ķ —Ā–į“õ—ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ where it should have been a clarifying question; (2) `–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –∂–į—Ā—č–ľ “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?` misclassified as `StatementOfAge` because the detector keyed on substring `–∂–į—Ā—č–ľ` and ran before `detect_ask_age`. Both fixed via a new `check_contradiction` template family + planner override and a question-particle guard with reordered detector dispatch. The cognitive contour was already correct in v4.4.0 ‚ÄĒ only the surface text and 1sg-self-recall classification leaked.

**v4.4.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ belief-poisoning recovery.** A v4.3.2 follow-on: once `BeliefState.contradictions` was non-empty for *any* reason ‚ÄĒ real conflict, transient typo, or upstream parse glitch ‚ÄĒ the planner clamped every subsequent turn to `CheckContradiction` with no clean exit. v4.4.0 adds two complementary escape hatches:

- **Explicit user-initiated dismissal.** New `BeliefState::dismiss_contradiction` (symmetric to v4.1.0 `resolve_contradiction`) supersedes both contested facts and clears the pending question. `Conversation::try_dismiss_pending_contradiction` fires on nine KZ phrases (`–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—É—Ė –ī–Ķ –∂–ĺ“õ`, `–Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ`, `“Ī–ľ—č—ā`, ‚Ä¶) ‚ÄĒ runs *before* resolution so a "–Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ" doesn't accidentally pick a candidate. New `Action::DismissContradiction` variant + `dismiss_contradiction` template family confirm the dismissal in plain Kazakh.
- **Implicit time-bounded priority cap.** New `ActionPlanner::CONTRADICTION_PRIORITY_TURNS = 3` + `plan_with_turn(...)` API. A conflict logged at turn `T` dominates `T`/`T+1`/`T+2`; on `T+3` it falls through to normal action paths. The conflict stays in `belief.contradictions` for audit ‚ÄĒ only planner priority changes.

**v4.3.0 milestone ‚ÄĒ language core, typed evidence, and ontology gates.** Three architectural layers landed in tandem:

- **Language Core** (`crates/adam-dialog/src/language_core.rs`) ‚ÄĒ orthography, mixed-script Latin/Cyrillic cleanup, proper-noun normalization, and **canonical entity resolution** for geography. Place mentions like `–ź–Ľ–ľ–į-–ź—ā–į`, `–£—Ā—ā—Ć-–ö–į–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ–ĺ–≥–ĺ—Ä—Ā–ļ`, `–ö–į—Ā–Ņ–ł–Ļ —ā–Ķ“£—Ė–∑—Ė` resolve to stable `geo_kz_NNN` ids from `data/world_core/geography_kz.jsonl`. Memory now stores entities by canonical id, not surface string.
- **Typed Evidence** (`ToolEvidence` in `crates/adam-dialog/src/tool.rs`) ‚ÄĒ `ToolResult` now carries machine-readable `Vec<ToolEvidence>` alongside textual `findings`, with variants `BeliefFact` / `GraphFact` / `RetrievalSample` / `DerivedFact { rule_id, support_chain }`. Higher layers verify *which typed claim* justifies a user-facing answer.
- **Ontology Gates** (`crates/adam-reasoning/src/ontology.rs`) ‚ÄĒ type constraints on admissible facts (rule-predicate match, place-object validation for spatial predicates, time-like validation for temporal predicates). Graph and reasoner consumers reject structurally invalid facts before verbalisation.
- **Quality Module** (`crates/adam-dialog/src/quality.rs`) ‚ÄĒ deterministic response-quality gate that audits every reply for placeholder leaks, Latin debug artifacts, surface-vs-trace faithfulness, and typed-evidence faithfulness.

**v4.2.0 milestone**: the dialog turn is a **data-driven tool-loop interpreter**. `Conversation::turn_with_trace` builds a `Vec<ToolCall>`, dispatches in one uniform pass, folds results back through `apply_tool_results`. The `inject_*` framing is retired; adding a new tool consult is a one-line append.

**v4.1.0 milestone**: cognitive eval reaches **22/22 canonical, 0 aspirational**. Kernel detects contradictions across turns, asks the user for resolution, revises belief state with full audit trail.

Three things make the trade viable specifically for Kazakh:

- **Agglutinative advantage** ‚ÄĒ Kazakh's rich morphology means the FST unpacks each word into a typed bundle (root + case + number + possessive + predicate-person), which the retrieval index and reasoner both exploit. What would be a 10‚Ā∂-parameter subword model in English is a 14 k-root Lexicon + deterministic rules here.
- **Mathematical determinism** ‚ÄĒ same input + same session + same seed produces a byte-identical answer across runs. No temperature, no sampling, no GPU.
- **No ungrounded generation by design** ‚ÄĒ every output is either a template realisation, a corpus quote, or a rule derivation with a full `source_chain`. There is no free-text generator anywhere in the pipeline that could invent content not traceable to its source.

| | adam v4.3 | mainstream LLM |
|---|---|---|
| Outputs | template + verbatim quote + FST synthesis + **rule-derived chain** | probabilistic token generation |
| Ungrounded generation | **none by construction** (retrieval quotes verbatim; reasoner derives only from typed facts) | non-zero, non-auditable |
| Inference | ms on laptop CPU | dollars on GPU / datacentre |
| **Reasoning** | **forward-chaining over typed facts, every conclusion has a `rule_id`** | opaque emergent reasoning |
| **Belief revision** | **explicit `BeliefState` with `Active`/`Superseded`/`Contested` lifecycle; user-driven contradiction resolution (v4.1.0)** | implicit, untraceable across turns |
| **Canonical entities (v4.3.0)** | **stable `geo_kz_NNN` ids resolved from `world_core/geography_kz.jsonl`; `–ź–Ľ–ľ–į-–ź—ā–į` / `–ö–į—Ā–Ņ–ł–Ļ —ā–Ķ“£—Ė–∑—Ė` / typo aliases all collapse to one canonical record** | string-keyed; memory drift across surface forms |
| **Typed evidence (v4.3.0)** | **`ToolResult.evidence: Vec<ToolEvidence>` carries `BeliefFact` / `GraphFact` / `RetrievalSample` / `DerivedFact { rule_id, support_chain }` per dispatch ‚ÄĒ every claim is auditable to its source class** | text-only, no machine-readable provenance |
| **Ontology gates (v4.3.0)** | **`adam_reasoning::ontology` validates rule-predicate matches, place-object types for spatial predicates, time-like types for temporal predicates** | none |
| **Response-quality audit (v4.3.0)** | **`audit_response` + `audit_trace_faithfulness` + `audit_typed_faithfulness` reject placeholder leaks, Latin debug artifacts, surface-vs-trace divergence, evidence-class mismatches** | none ‚ÄĒ generation isn't introspected |
| **Provenance** | **`source_chain: Vec<FactSource>` per derivation; `(pack, sample_id)` per quote; `Provenance::UserStatement { turn_id }` per belief fact; `EntityMemory.canonical_id` per remembered place** | ~none for free-form output |
| **Inference marker** | **¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā-¬Ľ on every reasoned claim, test-enforced** | ‚ÄĒ |
| **Stack policy** | **Rust-only + graph-first, contract-test enforced (no Python/JS/TS, no external graph DB, no Cypher/SPARQL)** | typically polyglot Python + neural runtime |
| Determinism | byte-identical across runs for same `(input, session, seed)` | temperature-dependent |
| Language coverage | Kazakh only | many, but shallow for low-resource |
| Knowledge depth | bounded by curated corpus + deterministic rules | broad, but fabricated edges |
| Self-improvement | ships by commit, reviewed by humans | parametric updates through training |

adam is **intentionally narrower** than an LLM. In return it is **predictable, cheap, safe, auditable, and ‚ÄĒ as of v4.1.0 ‚ÄĒ capable of holding conflicting beliefs simultaneously, surfacing them to the user, and revising them on demand**, while every conclusion carries a textual trust marker and every fact carries a source chain.

### Rust-Only Policy

The implementation language of `adam` is **Rust only**.

- No Python runtime.
- No Node / TypeScript runtime.
- No auxiliary model code in a second language.
- If the project needs a graph engine, verifier, trainer, retrieval index, or any other subsystem, it is either sourced from the Rust ecosystem or written in Rust inside this repository.
- POSIX shell wrappers in `scripts/` are allowed only as thin launchers around `cargo run` / `cargo test`; they must not introduce a second execution runtime.

This is a project invariant, not a preference. The repository carries contract tests that fail if non-Rust source files or foreign-language runtime invocations are introduced.

### Graph-First Policy

The graph layer of `adam` is **Rust-native and repository-native**.

- No external graph database as a required runtime.
- No Cypher / Gremlin / SPARQL query layer in the core pipeline.
- No Python graph stack (`networkx`, `igraph`, `graph-tool`) hidden behind scripts.
- The canonical graph representation, traversal, and artifact builders live in Rust crates and Rust binaries inside this repository.
- Shell scripts may orchestrate graph builds only as thin wrappers around `cargo run`.

This is also a repository invariant. Contract tests fail if a foreign graph stack is introduced or if the canonical Rust graph entrypoints disappear.

### Current state (v4.4.7 ‚ÄĒ honest numbers, verified 2026-04-27)

The cognitive contour shipped through v4.3.0 (language core, typed evidence, ontology gates, response-quality audit, stack policies) and v4.4.0 (belief-poisoning recovery: `Action::DismissContradiction` + contradiction-priority cap) remains the architectural baseline. v4.4.5‚Äďv4.4.7 added real-dialog adequacy fixes (`check_contradiction` template family + age/occupation 1sg-self-recall), the REPL replay battery, `CONTRIBUTING.md`, and a measurement / regression-policy layer. No new architectural layer in the v4.4.x patch series ‚ÄĒ those land at minor bumps.

Live numbers (verified 2026-04-29 against the actual repo): cognitive eval **65 / 65 canonical, 0 aspirational**. REPL replay: **69 / 69 canonical + 0 aspirational**. World Core: **1142 entries / 1305 curated facts across 33 domains**. Reasoner: **10 of 11 rules firing** with **23 418 derived facts** over **15 831 extracted + curated facts**. Morpheme index: **3 502 morphemes / 30 919 postings / 4 734 indexed samples** (incl. all 1 543 sentences across chapters 1‚Äď20 of the Rust Book Kazakh translation; per-pack ceiling lifted for rust_book at v4.7.21). Workspace: **745 tests passing**, 0 warnings. SystemAspect variants: **9** (General / Creator / Birthdate / Architecture / Capabilities / Knowledge / Limitations / Principles / SelfComparison). Template families: **59**. FST: **8 cases** (7 inflectional + 1 derivational LocativeAttributive at v4.5.0) √ó 2 numbers √ó 7 possessives √ó 7 predicate-person copulas; full synthesise / analyse round-trip across all four `-–ī–į“ď—č / -–ī–Ķ–≥—Ė / -—ā–į“ď—č / -—ā–Ķ–≥—Ė` allomorphs. Lexicon: **~25.5 k roots** (13 606 pure Kazakh + 11 919 Apertium imports). Every curated fact carries `ConfidenceKind::HumanApproved` with a named reviewer; every derivation has a `rule_id` + non-empty `source_chain`; every belief fact carries `Provenance` + `FactStatus`; every remembered place carries `EntityMemory.canonical_id`; every dialog turn's lookups are declared as `ToolCall`s and recorded as `ToolResult`s with typed `ToolEvidence` on `TurnTrace.tool_calls`. Nothing ungrounded leaves the deterministic recognised / grounded runtime path.

Single-active-fact invariant (v4.0.28) preserved across resolution; nothing is ever deleted |
